# Operation Log

Chronological record of significant operations. Each entry is its own file under `log/`; this page is the reverse-chronological index. See [concepts/parallel-session-coordination.md](concepts/parallel-session-coordination.md) for why.

- [2026-06-09 -- OLOS UI/UX trust copy: central copy module + 10 mentor-register rewords](log/2026-06-09-olos-uiux-copy-module.md) -- **Branch.** `main` (canonical; Phase 1+2 merged out-of-band `763415ee`). **Nothing pushed** ([[project-structured-capture-on-main]]). Implemented all 10 trust-building UI/UX suggestions from `OLOS_UIUX_Suggestions.md` (theme "This Thinks The Way I Think") across v3 Plan -> Act -> Observe, extracting every reworded user-facing string into a NEW central copy module `apps/web/src/v3/copy/` (barrel + `plan`/`act`/`observe`/`shared` + tests). Lives in **`apps/web`, NOT `packages/shared`** (React-surface chrome; shared stays UI-string-free). Static strings -> frozen consts; parameterized copy -> pure store-free functions (`revisionHeadline`, `revisionSupporting`, `domainUnansweredQuestion`, `feedsFallback`, `observeSignalConfirmation`, `decisionCount`); `DOMAIN_QUESTION` is a `Record<UniversalDomain,string>` exhaustive over all 16 domains (compiler- + test-enforced). Per suggestion: (1) language audit reword; (2) first-Plan-entry line; (3) `feedsFallback` "feeds into" chrome (authored `feedHint`/`feedNote` stay in seed); (4) visible Observe-signal confirmation on first Act task via existing `feedKey` (no new feed plumbing -- `appendObserveFeedFor` already emits; FieldAction has no `domainId` -> `null`); (5) mentor locked-popover; (6) site-survey unlock line (`'default'`; terrain auto-detect DEFERRED); (7) in-sheet post-divergence confirmation after `markDiverged`; (8) per-domain empty-state question on `DomainStatusCard` (the one card-shaped surface) + short `notYetRead` ("Not yet read") reword on the 5 compact "Not yet observed" cells; (9) ecological revision banner ("The land is asking you to look again"); (10) cycle-name echo (functions take a cycle title; `null` where not in scope -- future-cycle metrics DEFERRED). **Seed-data boundary held** -- only chrome templates moved; `feedsInto`/`feedHint`/`feedNote` stay in `packages/shared`. Double-quoted literals, ASCII-only. **Verified:** web `tsc` EXIT 0 (8GB heap); bounded `--pool=forks` ([[feedback-vitest-bounded-runs]]) copy-module pure fns + 16-domain exhaustiveness + null-cycle omission, DecisionWorkingPanel 55 + observeWiring 6, Observe/copy 264; full suite **4354 pass / 1 pre-existing fail**; lint (==typecheck) green; audit grep clean; DecisionWorkingPanel preview **screenshot** confirmed Act copy live (Observe dashboard NOT live-previewable -- dead dev API + no project, reported honestly per CLAUDE.md). **Flagged (not mine):** `workbenchAffordances.test.ts` `ev-s1-legal-governance` `showGroups` true-vs-false is a pre-existing out-of-band mismatch outside this change surface (concurrent S2 session owns those files). Amanah: pure land-stewardship copy -- no capital/sales/advance-purchase/financing, no riba/gharar/`bay' ma laysa 'indak`/CSRA/salam ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]], [[feedback-csa-in-catalogues]]). ADR [[decisions/2026-06-09-olos-uiux-copy-module]]; entities [[entities/act-tier-shell]], [[entities/observe-dashboard]]; concurrent [[log/2026-06-09-atlas-act-tier0-phase3a-land-reading]].
- [2026-06-08 -- Live-site login bypass via per-visitor demo sessions](log/2026-06-08-demo-mode-live-login-bypass.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/structured-capture-forms`. Live-site login (`atlas.ogden.ag`) is broken and the operator wants test users to explore without a login gate (which also overstates readiness). Frontend gate is a trivial `localStorage` token check, but the **backend enforces JWT on ~every route with no env bypass** -- so removing the gate alone would 401 everywhere. **Fix:** behind build-time flag `FEATURE_DEMO_MODE` (default off; on only for the live web build), auto-register a unique throwaway account (`guest-<uuid>@demo.ogden.ag`) on boot when no token exists, reusing the already-open `register` endpoint -- **zero backend changes**. Operator-confirmed: auto demo session (land straight in app) / keep login reachable (`/login` still works) / per-visitor throwaway accounts. NEW `app/demoSession.ts` (`DEMO_MODE_ENABLED`, `makeGuestCredentials`, `isDemoUser`, `maybeBootDemoSession` raced against a 1500ms timeout, errors swallowed) + `bootAuthed.ts` hook + `AppShell` three-way control (**DEMO MODE** badge + **Sign in**->`/login` for demo users) + `vite.config.ts` define + `.env.example` + `Dockerfile.nginx` ARG/ENV + `render.yaml` `FEATURE_DEMO_MODE: "true"` (**the live toggle**) + launch.json web-demo. Entirely flag-gated, so **OFF == original landing/login by construction** (terser dead-code-eliminates the demo path). **Verified** on two fresh prod builds (temp `preview.proxy`, reverted): bundle fold ON `!0` / OFF `!1`, 0 unreplaced survivals; demo-ON E2E auto-registered `guest-...@demo.ogden.ag` (7-day JWT) -> `/v3/portfolio`, **DEMO MODE** badge + Sign in, 4 projects incl. 351 House (12 ha) live, no 401s (**screenshot**); demo-OFF regression token absent / public landing / no badge (**screenshot**); 11 bounded `--pool=forks` unit tests pass ([[feedback-vitest-bounded-runs]]); web `tsc` clean. Deferred: demo-user DB cleanup job, optional verification-email skip for the demo domain, the underlying real-login fix. Amanah: access/onboarding only -- no sale/financing/CSRA ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]]). ADR [[decisions/2026-06-08-atlas-demo-mode-per-visitor-sessions]]; entity [[entities/web-app]].
- [2026-06-08 -- Parcel area displayed ~2.47x too high: unit convention fix](log/2026-06-08-parcel-area-unit-fix.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/structured-capture-forms` (**pushed**). Fixed metric project areas overstated ~2.47x due to `LocalProject.acreage` (canonically ACRES from the API) being relabeled as "ha" without conversion by four display/adapter paths, and stored as unit-native ha by four write paths (causing ha/acres flip-flop on sync). **Fix:** added `parcelAcres(geo)` / `parcelAreaValue(acres, units)` / `formatParcelArea(acres, units)` helpers to `geo.ts`; write paths (`ObserveLayout`, `PlanLayout`, `ActLayout`, `WizardStep1Site`) now call `parcelAcres()` (always stores acres); read paths (`ArchivePage`, `PortfolioSummaryBar`, `projectToCandidate`, `adaptLocalProject`, `pdfExport`) convert via the new helpers. **Verified:** 30/30 geo tests; typecheck clean; live preview Halton Hills 122.22 ac -> 49.46 ha (was 122.2 ha). Amanah: area measurement, no sales instrument ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]]). ADR [[decisions/2026-06-08-atlas-parcel-area-unit-fix]].

Flags (no change): **row-15 prototype-file mismatch** (`olos_communal_infra_strategy.html` carries nursery content; catalogue `ev-s4-infra-strategy` verified correct, file needs re-export) + a **4-item covenant-content inventory** (faith/halal/financial right-panel provisions with no catalogue home, for operator review). Amanah: row-21 member cost-sharing CLEAN -- no riba, no `bay` ma laysa `indak`/CSRA/salam ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]], [[feedback-csa-in-catalogues]]). Deferred: bespoke Tier-1+ work surfaces + mode badges, covenant-provision promotion decision, prototype re-export. - [2026-06-06 -- Tier-0 Stakeholders surface (Phase C Part 3, sub-project 2 of 3: shared register + cultural Amanah item)](log/2026-06-06-atlas-tier0-stakeholders.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/structured-capture-forms` (clean explicit-path commits `8f4b0bad`/`f676ba49`/`3849c8cd`(+tidy `e6e86c27`)/`7f5ba370`/`684192de`/`f645ad45` for ST1-ST6, then mockup-reconciliation `6d7005d5`/`e6ee4984`/`4c076105`/`41ddc7da` for SR-A..SR-D; **not pushed**). Widened the Tier-0 workbench from `s1-vision`+`s1-boundaries` to also cover **`s1-stakeholders`** ("A mapped picture of stakeholders & community", 6 mandatory items c1-c6 in two groups), building the capture from the operator mockup `olos_stakeholders_mixed_surface.html`. Second of THREE sequenced sub-projects (Boundaries [shipped] -> Stakeholders -> Stewards); Stewards (RBAC/invite) deferred to its own plan. **The first Tier-0 surface whose authoritative state is a project-level SHARED REGISTER, not per-item `FormValue`** -- items 1-4 build a register of stakeholder records, items 5-6 annotate the same records. That departure drove the core design choice. **Builds on / reuses (does NOT rebuild)** the Tier-0 workbench + working panel + the per-item completion/rationale/defer path + the threaded `resolveOptions` prop + `DecisionList` `modeFor` badges. **Architecture (additive, no deletion):** **(1) Option A -- store-direct capture, panel keeps the completion marker** -- `StakeholderCapture` subscribes to the new `stakeholderRegisterStore` directly and does register CRUD inline; the panel's per-item `FormValue` + `onRecord` degrade to a thin per-item completion MARKER that still flows through `actEvidenceStore` (`saveVisionFormData` + `setItemComplete`); capture owns register I/O, panel owns completion + rationale + defer; **(2) Zustand v5 stable-snapshot trap (the #1 risk) fixed by construction** -- reactive consumers (panel validity, workbench reg-strip count) select the STABLE raw object `s.byProject[projectId] ?? EMPTY_STAKEHOLDERS_BY_ID` (frozen constant) and derive the array/count via `useMemo` -- never a fresh-array `listForProject` selector (which would infinite-loop); pure helpers take a register snapshot; **(3) one shared `StakeholderRecord` register store** -- NEW `apps/web/src/store/stakeholderRegisterStore.ts` mirroring `proofRecordStore.ts` minus api/sync: `byProject[projectId][id]`, create/update/delete/list/get, verbatim private `mutate`, persist `ogden-stakeholder-register` v2 + partialize byProject, frozen `EMPTY_STAKEHOLDERS_BY_ID`; **(4) c3 mandatory NON-DEFERRABLE (Amanah)** -- `DecisionPanelTarget` gains `deferrable?: boolean`; `buildDecisionTarget` sets it `false` only for `s1-stakeholders-c3`; the footer hides defer when `deferrable === false`; c3 is ALWAYS valid and records a 5-status cultural model (`not-investigated` default, `enquiry-no-obligations`, `active-consultation`, `assessment-required`, `formal-protocol`) + notes in the marker -- silence is never completion; **(5) per-item modes + validity decoupled from completion** -- `stakeholderModeFor`: c1 `mapContact`, c2 `contact`, c3 `cultural`, c4 `contact`, c5/c6 `annotate`; post-mockup only c1 (>=1 neighbour) and c2 (>=1 authority) can be invalid, c3/c4/c5/c6 always valid (old "none toggle" escape-hatch removed); `recorded` comes from the per-item marker NOT row counts, capture keyed on itemId so switching items never loses register state; **(6) workbench strips + badges + predicate** -- two strips render for `s1-stakeholders` only (static map-strip "2 overlays active on map" + LIVE reg-strip with count via the stable-snapshot pattern, "stakeholders in register", ASCII note "Items 1-4 build the register - Items 5-6 annotate it"), `DecisionList.MODE_LABELS` extended with the 4 stakeholder labels, `ActTierShell` adds `'s1-stakeholders'` to `TIER_ZERO_OBJECTIVE_IDS`; **(7) options via the already-threaded `resolveOptions` prop** -- `_base`-only stakeholder sets in `FIELD_OPTION_SETS`, content reconciled verbatim to the mockup (SR-A), no new resolver. **ST1 `8f4b0bad`:** stakeholder `_base`-only option sets + tests; First of THREE sequenced sub-projects (Boundaries -> Stakeholders -> Stewards); the latter two deferred to their own plans. **Builds on / reuses (does NOT rebuild)** the Tier-0 workbench + working panel + `actEvidenceStore.visionFormData` persistence ([[log/2026-06-06-atlas-tier0-vision-classify]]). **Architecture (additive, no deletion):** **(1) one mode-routing bespoke component, not six arms** -- `DecisionWorkingPanel` adds ONE flag (`isBoundary`) + ONE body-router arm delegating to a self-routing `BoundaryCapture` that switches on `itemId` internally (mirrors how vision-classify/labour each add one arm; the 4 modes + 7 ids stay co-located); **(2) capture data now, defer rich I/O** (operator decision) -- map pin/draw is a static decorative inline SVG + a **disabled "Open map -- coming soon"** affordance (no MapboxGL in the workbench, no nav), file upload is a **metadata-only stub** (`onChange` sets a placeholder `docName`; no file read/storage), every "Open map"/"Pin easement"/"Draw ROW line" control rendered `disabled`; **(3) all 7 items persist through the UNCHANGED flat `FormValue`** on the EXISTING `visionFormData[itemId]` slice -- `BoundaryCapture` reasons with a typed `BoundaryModel` (discriminated union by `kind`: c1 titleDeed/doc, c2 map, c3 easement/mapEntry, c4 zoning/decision, c5 water/decision, c6 covenant/doc, c7 permits/decision) but `encodeBoundary`/`decodeBoundary` round-trip losslessly (only non-string field `acknowledged` encoded `'true'|''`; water `entitlement` stored as its raw string), `decodeBoundary` is TOTAL (safe per-mode defaults; unknown id -> map default); **no store change/migration**; **(4) options via the already-threaded `resolveOptions` prop** -- 10 `_base`-only sets added to `FIELD_OPTION_SETS` (`boundaryDocStatus`, `boundaryZoning` (7), `boundaryPermittedUses`, `boundaryZoningReview`, `boundaryWaterSources`, `boundaryWaterUnit` ML/kL/m3, `boundaryWaterStatus`, `boundaryEasementImplications`, `boundaryCovenantTypes`, `boundaryPermitActivities`; REVIEW-flagged, verbatim from the mockup), **no new resolver** (boundary options do not vary by project type); **(5) bespoke validity/summary derived once, routed BEFORE `hasFields`** -- `boundaryModel` decoded once + reused across validity (`isBoundaryValid(itemId, model)` -- per-mode required fields; helpers take `(itemId, model)` since the model carries the `kind` discriminant; no `fields` collision because `s1-boundaries-c*` have NO form tool; **(6) detection + badges + map strip** -- `buildDecisionTarget` sets `isBoundary = item.id.startsWith('s1-boundaries-')`, `DecisionList` gains optional `modeFor` mode badges (Document/Map/Map+entry/Decision; absent for s1-vision), workbench renders a static map-activation strip ("2 overlays will activate on the map: Risk / Compliance, Site Boundary") for s1-boundaries only; **(7) predicate widened incrementally** -- `ActTierShell` replaces the single `TIER_ZERO_OBJECTIVE_ID = 's1-vision'` with a membership Set `TIER_ZERO_OBJECTIVE_IDS = {'s1-vision','s1-boundaries'}`, both predicates (`isTierZeroObjective`, `isTierZeroObjectiveId`) test `.has(...)` (purely additive; map shell + modal suppression already key off these predicates, map render path byte-unchanged; deferred I/O means the workbench is fully self-contained for s1-boundaries -- the map shell simply stops mounting, exactly as for s1-vision). **BT1 `381a7455`:** 10 `_base`-only boundary option sets; - [2026-06-06 -- Tier-0 Vision-classify surface (Phase C Part 2: bespoke committed/aspirational sort)](log/2026-06-06-atlas-tier0-vision-classify.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/structured-capture-forms` (clean explicit-path commits `6c736503`/`65b3ef2a`/`468421db`/`63724014`/`79e78e14`/`aea42348`/`6b5ab59c`/`428717e7`; **not pushed**). Replaced the **generic** `VisionFormFields` rendering of the `s1-vision-classify` Tier-0 decision with a **bespoke surface** that sorts candidate **vision elements** into two columns -- **Committed** (do now) vs **Aspirational** (longer-horizon) -- via type-aware suggestion chips, a **transient Unclassified staging zone**, a write-your-own input with a committed/aspirational role toggle, in-column switch/delete, and a show-more toggle. Follows the Phase-B `SuccessCriteriaCapture` + Phase-C-Part-1 `LabourInventoryCapture` controlled-renderer pattern; **builds on / reuses (does NOT rebuild)** the Tier-0 workbench + working panel ([[log/2026-06-06-atlas-tier0-labour-surface]]). **Architecture (additive, no deletion):** **(1) byte-compatible value -- NO encode** -- the value shape `{ committed: string[]; aspirational: string[] }` is already NATIVE `FormValue` (both arms plain `string[]`, the SAME shape the existing form tool persists), so `decodeClassify` is a TOTAL read (non-array -> `[]`; non-string elements filtered, `[1,null,'x'] -> ['x']`) with no inverse encode, `onChange` writes the two arrays straight back; **(2) transient Unclassified staging is component-local UI, NEVER persisted** -- a staged chip lives only in `useState` until the steward sorts it into a column, `inUse(text)` enforces text-uniqueness across all three lists; **(3) type-aware suggestions via shared `resolveVisionClassifyOptions(primary, secondaries)`** (mirrors the `resolveLabourSkills`/`resolveSuccessCriteriaOptions` union/dedup/order idiom; starter `VISION_CLASSIFY_OPTIONS` REVIEW-flagged) -- **plain strings, NOT domain-tagged** (the committed/aspirational axis is the steward's sort-time judgement, not a design-time tag); **(4) bespoke validity/summary routed FIRST** (before labour/success-criteria/`hasFields`/textarea) -- `isVisionClassifyValid` (`committed.length + aspirational.length >= 1`) + `summariseVisionClassify` ("N committed, M aspirational"), NOT the generic `isFormValueValid`/`summariseFormValue`; the draft is decoded ONCE into a single `classifyModel` reused by validity/summary/body (mirrors labour `labourModel`); the early arm is **load-bearing** because `s1-vision-classify` DOES match a form tool (would otherwise fall through to the generic renderer); **(5) detection** -- `buildDecisionTarget` flags `isVisionClassify` directly via `item.id === 's1-vision-classify'` (simpler than labour's tool-formId join, dependency-free), the workbench resolves suggestions inline (no-memo) + threads them via the new `visionClassifySuggestions` panel prop (the vision-classify form tool + its `fields` stay in `actToolCatalog.ts` as the modal/`<select>` fallback). **VC1 `6c736503` (+polish `65b3ef2a`):** NEW `VISION_CLASSIFY_OPTIONS` + `resolveVisionClassifyOptions` resolver (REVIEW-flagged starter list; polish disambiguated the staging discard aria-label (`Remove "<text>" from staging`, fixing a JSDOM accessible-name collision) + added garbage-decode/switch-column tests. **VC2 baseline `79e78e14`:** restored the clean web-tsc baseline -- a prior LC4-test tweak left `getAllByText(expected[0])` (`string|undefined`) failing tsc though vitest passed; - [2026-06-06 -- Tier-0 cold-load map-flicker fix + Phase B live smoke PASSES](log/2026-06-06-atlas-tier0-cold-load-map-flicker-fix.md) -- **Closes the one remaining Phase B verification gate.** Fix commit `a842f3f2` (`fix(act): gate Tier-0 swap on URL objectiveId to avoid cold-load map mount`; 2 files: `ActTierShell.tsx` + `.module.css`; local-only, not pushed). **Root cause (confirmed):** `ActTierShell.tsx:768` read `showTierZeroWorkbench = selectedObjective != null && isTierZeroObjective(selectedObjective)`; `selectedObjective` derives from async-hydrated `objectives`, so on a COLD deep-link to `/v3/project/<id>/act/tier-shell/s1-vision` it is briefly `null` and the shell transiently mounted `<StageShell>` -> `<DiagnoseMap>` (MapboxGL/WebGL) -- a brief flicker in a real browser, but it **permanently wedges the headless preview renderer**, which is what blocked the Phase B smoke. **Fix (additive, scoped):** gate the swap on the URL-synchronous `objectiveId` (`isTierZeroObjectiveId(objectiveId) || (selectedObjective != null && isTierZeroObjective(selectedObjective))`) so the workbench wins from the first render; a non-map `.tierZeroLoading` placeholder (`role="status"`) covers the pre-hydration window; `<StageShell>`/`<DiagnoseMap>` is never reached on `s1-vision`, and the spatial map path is byte-unchanged. **Verified:** web `tsc` EXIT 0; bounded vitest green (5 pre-existing `actWorkItemModule` failures proven unrelated by stash-out/in); **live smoke now GREEN** -- client-side nav AND hard reload (the cold path that used to wedge) at `/v3/project/mtc/act/tier-shell/s1-vision` both reach `readyState: complete` with **0 canvases / 0 mapbox elements** and the workbench rendered (**screenshot captured**). **Side-finding:** the suspected "/home reload loop" was a **preview-tool artifact, not an app bug** -- client-side nav to `/home` returns full DOM in ~4s (a blocked thread would time out); once one map mount wedges the shared headless WebGL context, every subsequent hard nav (incl. map-free `/home`) appears to hang because the renderer is dead. Modified auth pages (`isAuthenticated()`/`beforeLoad` does NOT ping-pong) and the catalogue spine-gate WIP (bounded status engine) **exonerated**; no code change from that investigation. Explicit-pathspec commit (2 files); foreign WIP NEVER staged/touched ([[project-branch-rebase]], [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]], [[feedback-no-deletion]]); not pushed; ASCII-only. - [2026-06-05 -- Act: wire [service threshold] trigger recognition end-to-end](log/2026-06-05-atlas-act-service-threshold-trigger.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (clean explicit-path commit `e3d31167`, 5 files +84/−16; **not pushed**). Fixed three silent gaps that prevented `u-s5-infrastructure-failure` (`[service threshold]` universal protocol) from ever surfacing the `TriggerRecognitionSheet` in Act. **Gap 1:** `FEEDS_TO_MODULE` was missing `'Built Infrastructure' → 'built-infrastructure'`; `pickTrigger()` matches via `t.feeds.some(f => FEEDS_TO_MODULE[f] === domainId)` — without this entry the protocol was permanently invisible. **Gap 2:** The `triggerTemplates` useMemo only called `templatesForEnterprises()` — universal templates (no `enterpriseScope`) always returned `false` for the enterprise-scope `.some()` check and were silently excluded; fixed by concatenating `UNIVERSAL_PROTOCOL_TEMPLATES` (also exported from `@ogden/shared` barrel — was only in catalogues sub-index). **Gap 3:** `TriggerRecognitionSheet` was passed base `outputs` rather than `outputsFor(pendingTrigger.id)`, so `[service threshold]` stayed unresolved even after the threshold editor wrote a value; fixed by destructuring `outputsFor` and passing `outputsFor(pendingTrigger.id)`. Also reordered `s3-systems-baseline` in `objectiveObserveDomains.ts` to put `'built-infrastructure'` first — `getPrimaryDomainForObjective` returns `domains[0]`, and checklist c3 ("Note existing infrastructure") is semantically the primary output. **Verified:** 6/6 bounded `--pool=forks` tests (new describe block confirms Infrastructure Failure trigger sheet surfaces on built-infrastructure objective); `tsc` EXIT 0; live DOM: Infrastructure Failure card shows `data-protocol-status="active"` in S5 Protocol Layer + **screenshot** (full trigger-sheet path not demonstrable via MTC UI — MTC has no built-infrastructure enterprise objective in its Act view; path verified through test suite). Explicit-pathspec `git commit -F` of exactly 5 files; not pushed ([[project-branch-rebase]], [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]); Amanah -- structural monitoring, no sales instrument ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]]). entity [[entities/act-tier-shell]].

- [2026-06-03 -- Closed-loop Plan->Act workflow: Slice A4 (approval gate + Act handoff contract)](log/2026-06-03-atlas-closed-loop-slice-a4.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (explicit-path commit `627503e9`, 8 files; **not pushed**). Fifth and **FINAL** slice of Phase A of the multi-session Plan->Act closed-loop workflow -- it defines the cross-phase data contract Phase B consumes, gates approval, and previews + triggers the enrichment onto the EXISTING `ActHandoffPackage` WITHOUT a schema change and WITHOUT a second handoff path. NEW pure `features/plan/closedLoop/loopApprovalGate.ts`: `canApproveLoop(validation, allowOrphanOutputs) -> { ok, counts, reason }`; blocking order (first failure wins) empty flows -> dangling endpoints (null source OR sink) -> orphan fertility (no flow in/out; blocks even with the escape hatch) -> orphan outputs (`fertilityWithoutFeedstock`) unless `allowOrphanOutputs`; mirrors the existing `getAllowOrphanOutputs(project)` escape-hatch precedent (there is no `statusGate.ts`). NEW pure `features/plan/closedLoop/loopHandoffContract.ts` -- THE cross-phase contract: `buildLoopActPayload(project, flows, infra, validation)` maps the `MaterialFlow` design onto the EXISTING `ActHandoffPackageSchema` (throughput -> one material per flow, dominant unit kg/month > L/month > kWh/month; per-flow cadence -> monitoring requirements via `cadenceLabel`; closed flows -> success criteria; source->via...->sink graph -> topology-ordered `sequence`, upstream-first, pure cycles broken deterministically in stable input order) -> returns `Partial<ActHandoffPackage>` (four enriched arrays + a `workScope` summary; id/projectId/planDecisionRecordId/createdAt stay with the store's `createPackage`) + a `LoopActSummary` for the preview. NEW read-only `ActHandoffPreviewPanel.tsx` (+`.module.css`): "what approval will generate" -- the gate verdict chip + reason, a counts row (flows / closed-loop / dangling / orphan outputs with warn cues), the workScope, and four preview lists; all logic in the two tested helpers. TRIGGER: additive, domain-guarded (`objective.domain === "soil"`) branch in the EXISTING `v3/olos/handoff/PlanToActHandoff.tsx` `onEmit` -- when the domain matches, `buildLoopActPayload({ id: projectId }, loopFlows, loopInfra, loopValidation).payload` enriches the `createPackage` args; every other domain keeps today's empty arrays (single handoff path). Hook reads unconditional; `useClosedLoopValidation` fed a minimal `{ id: projectId } as LocalProject` stub because the hook reads ONLY `project.id` (verified), keeping the call legal under the Rules of Hooks. LAYOUT: a third "Loop / Handoff" tab on `WasteVectorTool.tsx` rendering the preview (reuses module routing; NO new route, NO StageShell slot). **Verified:** shared `tsc --noEmit` EXIT 0; web `tsc --noEmit` (with `--max-old-space-size=8192`) reports ONLY the 2 untracked foreign-WIP `src/compost/ObserveStage.tsx` errors (`??`, externally rebased in, [[project-branch-rebase]]) -- my 8 files produce zero errors; the closedLoop suite **53/53** green bounded `--pool=forks --testTimeout=20000` (loopApprovalGate 6 + loopHandoffContract 7 added to the prior 40) ([[feedback-vitest-bounded-runs]]). **Live render-verify deferred (honesty gate):** the new tab lives inside `WasteVectorTool` -- the same legacy `PlanModuleSlideUp` "soil" host A1/A2/A3 found unreachable through the current strata-spine IA via automation; adding the tab did not change that reachability, so the panel + the end-to-end emit were NOT exercised on a live MTC surface this slice; evidence basis is the 53/53 unit suite + clean shared/web typecheck, disclosed not claimed ([[project-screenshot-hang]]). The deferred Phase-A live-verify now depends on a separate strata-IA route to `WasteVectorTool`. - [2026-05-29 -- Plan Tier detail-panel: hide MAP ACTIVATION section when no overlays bound](log/2026-05-29-plan-tier-detail-panel-hide-empty-map.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (1 file: `apps/web/src/v3/plan/tiers/ObjectiveDetailPanel.tsx`). JSX-only follow-up to [[decisions/2026-05-27-atlas-plan-tier-shell-phase1]] Slice 1.6. Steward flagged a screenshot of the ObjectiveDetailPanel showing the "MAP ACTIVATION" strip empty-state ("No overlays bound to this objective.") with a 260px satellite map still rendering underneath -- *"why is the map view here? It should not be."* Root cause: `MapActivationStrip` + `<div className={css.mapBody}><ObjectiveMap/></div>` rendered **unconditionally**, while only the strip's message gated on `objective.defaultOverlayBundle.length === 0` (inside OLOS `OverlayBundleStrip`); all 8 seeded objectives have `defaultOverlayBundle: []`, so an empty strip + a pointless map showed on every objective. Fix: derive `const hasOverlays = objective.defaultOverlayBundle.length > 0` and wrap the strip + map in `{hasOverlays && (<>...</>)}` -- the exact inverse of the empty-state condition, so the **whole** MAP ACTIVATION region (eyebrow + message + map) unmounts when no overlays are bound (steward-confirmed scope via AskUserQuestion) and reappears once a bundle is non-empty. Gated on `defaultOverlayBundle` not `activeOverlayIds` (stays visible while toggling individual overlays). Out of scope: `MapActivationStrip`/`OverlayBundleStrip` untouched (shared with `ObjectiveWorkspace`, [[feedback-no-deletion]]); no seed change; no CSS change (`.panel` has no `gap`, so removal leaves none). **Verified:** `tsc --noEmit` exit 0 / empty output (clean, no new errors); live `preview_eval` on project `d2708c91` across both panel states -- `t0-vision` (COMPLETE + review banner) and `t1-land-baseline` (READY, no banner) both show `_mapBody`, map canvas, "Map activation" eyebrow, and "No overlays bound" message all absent, panel flowing header -> (banner) -> YOUR DECISIONS with no gap; **screenshot captured** this session (tab visible, `document.hidden === false` -- unlike the sibling column-width task). Reappearance case sound by construction (bundled const not runtime-mutable; guard is the boolean inverse of the proven empty-state). No ADR (visibility tweak too narrow; precedent the sibling entry + `1bc907d4` / `a6ee7ae8`). Explicit-path commit (3 files, mirrors `63459f5f`); foreign WIP from parallel sessions left out per [[feedback-no-deletion]]; divergence-checked before push per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]. CSRA model untouched; ASCII-only copy.

- [2026-05-29 -- projectType normalization: stop project:create 422ing on sync](log/2026-05-29-projecttype-normalization-422-fix.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (commit `fe367966`, 3 files: `store/projectStore.ts`, `lib/syncQueue.ts`, `lib/syncService.ts`). Continuation of the [[2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix]] thread: that fix bounded the sync queue so a permanently-failing op could no longer OOM the renderer, but left the *cause* of the validation failures unfixed and unnamed (the client discarded the server's `details[]`). This session root-caused it -- OLOS carries two project-type vocabularies, kebab-case **archetype** (`regenerative-farm`, `v3/true-north/trueNorthConfig.ts`) and the snake_case server **`projectType`** (`regenerative_farm`, the Zod `ProjectType` enum); `createProject` persisted the raw value, so a kebab archetype could leak in and `project:create` 422'd on sync, the circuit breaker then dropping the op (unsyncable on-device). Live diagnosis named the offender as **"Phase 4 Smoke"** (`regenerative-farm`) -- correcting the 2026-05-25 ADR's provisional "Moontrance Creek" / "Test Vision Project" attribution (Moontrance Creek is `projectType: null` / valid; "Test Vision Project" was a transient vision-builder fixture, [[2026-05-25-atlas-stage-zero-vision-builder]]); a dated `> [!warning] Correction` callout was added there. **Three-tier fix:** persist `migrate` v4 -> v5 repairs existing records via `normalizeProjectType` (kebab archetype -> enum via `ARCHETYPE_TO_PROJECT_TYPE`, valid pass-through, unknown -> syncable null); `createProject` normalizes on write (prevent recurrence); `describeSyncError` folds the server `details: [{ path, message }]` into `op.lastError` + the create-failure log (so the next 422 names the field). **Verified:** web `tsc --noEmit` clean; live `ogden-projects` migrated to version 5 with 0 schema offenders across 40 projects (typeCounts `{ "(null)": 4, homestead: 9, multi_enterprise: 16, regenerative_farm: 11 }`), clean projects untouched; `git diff --cached --name-only` confirmed only the 3 source files staged. **Carry-over (corrected 2026-05-29):** the [[2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix]] handler-swallow deferral was already closed the same day by [[decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-sync-circuit-breaker]] (`84bb8e91`) -- `executeQueuedOp` rethrows so `flush()` counts retries and drops exhausted ops via `handleExhaustedOp`; `describeSyncError` (this slice) makes such a drop name the offending field. Genuinely-open deferral: the human-gated two-device E2E + `FEATURE_SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` rollout. Not pushed (out-of-band rebase rule). ADR [[decisions/2026-05-29-atlas-projecttype-normalization-422-fix]]; corrects [[decisions/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix]]; CSRA model untouched; ASCII-only copy.

- [2026-05-28 — Scoped Views Epic design pass (Phase 5 Slice 5.5 re-scope)](log/2026-05-28-scoped-views-epic-design.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. **Design-only — no implementation code.** Re-scoped the one-line "Slice 5.5 — Contractor/Landowner scoped views (frontend-only, hook signature unchanged)" carry-over from [[log/2026-05-28-per-project-home-slice54]] into a **four-slice epic** after reading the ratified `OLOS_Project_Home_Spec_v1` (sections 1.3/4/5/6/7/8) against the code. The literal carry-over collapsed on three walls — (1) `memberStore.myRole` is a single slot (no per-project role map to filter a portfolio on), (2) `useProjectRole` only fetches when logged in + Portfolio Home reads the localStorage store, so a naive role filter empties the portfolio in the dominant offline/demo mode, (3) frontend filtering is not the spec's data-layer 403 (7.2/8.5) — and the spec is itself an epic (section 5 contractor task-only view, section 6 landowner read-only shareable progress view, section 7 contractor access expiry). Two verifications de-risked it: the API already gates ~every route on `authenticate -> resolveProjectRole -> requireRole(...)` (~22 callsites per `rbac.ts`), and the landowner view has a real foundation in the existing `v3/observe/dashboard/presentation/` suite + `presentationShareStore` + `ObserveShareViewerPage` + the `portal/` public-link API. Sharpest enforcement finding: `contractor` currently aliases to `designer` (`projectRoleCapabilities.ts:158`) with `{read, comment, edit}` over the whole project, so a contractor session satisfies every `requireRole('owner', 'designer')` gate today — full Plan/Observe access (Slice 5.1 flagged this as a deliberate placeholder pending "future Phase 5 slices"; 5.5a/5.5c own breaking it). **Three decisions locked via AskUserQuestion:** (1) re-scope as epic + design first (vs. ship a narrow frontend slice / build substrate then filter); (2) foundational principle — scoped views are an **authenticated + synced** capability, local-only/offline always renders full single-owner view (rejected: mandatory backend-backing; mirroring roles into the local store); (3) view order **Team -> Contractor -> Landowner** (steady risk ramp), with 5.5a (role substrate + enforcement spine) fixed first. **Roadmap:** 5.5a `useMyProjectRoles` bulk hook + Per-Project Home access gate + Portfolio role-filter (no-op offline) + break contractor Plan/Observe equivalence (403) -> 5.5b team-member assignment-scoped Per-Project Home -> 5.5c contractor task-only view + data-layer query scoping -> 5.5d landowner read-only progress view (on the presentation/portal substrate) + contractor access expiry (task-complete / manual / 90-day). Hook signature unchanged — the one surviving piece of the original carry-over. **Verified:** design-only (no tsc / vitest / preview); spec self-review passed (no placeholders, internally consistent, scoped, sole ambiguity — contractor enforcement mechanism — explicitly deferred to the 5.5a plan); `git diff --cached --name-only` confirmed exactly 4 wiki files staged (ADR + this log entry + index.md + log.md pointers), no foreign WIP from the exclusion list. **Immediate next:** Slice 5.5a implementation plan + execution; 5.5b-d each depend on 5.5a's substrate. ADR [[decisions/2026-05-28-atlas-scoped-views-epic-design]]; continues [[log/2026-05-28-per-project-home-slice54]]; no-deletion; 3-item nav forward IA ([[project-lifecycle-retirement]]); CSRA model untouched; ASCII-only copy.
- [2026-05-28 — Per-Project Home (Phase 5 Slice 5.4)](log/2026-05-28-per-project-home-slice54.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`5b463ef0`, 10 files +1267/−82). Shipped Phase 5 Slice 5.4 of the OLOS UX spec as a single explicit-path commit: the canonical **Per-Project Home** mounted at **both** `/v3/project/$projectId/home` (canonical landing) **and** `/v3/project/$projectId/` (default project route, no `home` suffix) so deep links and the default landing converge on the same `PerProjectHomePage` component, replacing the legacy `V3HomePage` mount on `v3IndexRoute`+`v3HomeRoute` (V3HomePage preserved on disk + import per [[feedback-no-deletion]] for Phase 7 retirement). The surface is composed of three regions per the Slice 5.3 ADR carry-over contract: **NextUpCard** (priority router that walks `urgency.breakdown` channels in descending severity — draft wizard → "Resume the project wizard" / critical divergence → "1 critical field divergence to review" → high divergence → "N field divergences to review" → stale foundation → "N foundation domains need fresh data" → cyclical review due → "Decision review due" → blocked field actions → field action fallback via `getNextUpForProject` → "Nothing urgent — land is steady." with no CTA), **AttentionRail** (vertical chip list keyed off the shared `buildUrgencyChips(urgency)` helper, one chip per non-zero breakdown channel — excluding `draftWizard` which is rendered as a separate "Finish setup" pill in the header — with empty state "No urgent signals. Land is steady."), and **StageStatusRow** (three `BentoBox` cards summarising Plan tier objective status via `computeAllObjectiveStatuses(PLAN_TIER_OBJECTIVES, toProgressMap(progress))`, field action counts via `useFieldActionStore.byProject[projectId]`, and foundation domain freshness via `computeDomainFreshness(points, nowMs, OBSERVE_DOMAIN_CATALOG[d].freshnessThresholds)` over `FOUNDATION_DOMAINS_FOR_REVISION` — Hydrology, Soil, Risk). The composing **`useProjectUrgency([project])`** hook from Slice 5.3 is consumed in **single-project mode** — the hook handles arbitrary array lengths with referentially-stable `Map<projectId, ProjectUrgencyResult>` returns, so the one-element case requires zero new substrate; the page reads `urgencyMap.get(project.id)` and threads `urgency` into NextUpCard + AttentionRail while StageStatusRow reads producer stores directly (it is not an urgency consumer). The urgency score is **never rendered** anywhere on the surface — NextUpCard uses it only as a structural tie-break inside its priority router (and even then the router orders branches by severity first, so the score rarely load-bears), AttentionRail surfaces breakdown channels as chips, StageStatusRow surfaces producer state directly; three roles, one canonical urgency reader, one canonical chip helper. The shared **`buildUrgencyChips` helper** was extracted from Slice 5.3's inlined `buildChips` into `apps/web/src/v3/home/urgencyChips.ts` so Portfolio Home and Per-Project Home cannot drift in copy or tone assignment as the urgency breakdown shape evolves; `ProjectUrgencyCard` adopts the helper (deletes 83 lines of inlined chip logic + types, adds the import + same rendering — rendered markup byte-identical to Slice 5.3 by construction). - [2026-05-25 — Command Centre shell: stop tray cutoff & rail blowout](log/2026-05-25-command-centre-shell-bounding.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`2368e687`, 1 file +17/−1). The Act Command Centre's bottom **"Open Work Items"** carousel rendered clipped at the viewport bottom, but **only** on the **All Modules** / **Tracker** tabs; a first attempt (`53a0e7a0` carousel `overflow-y:hidden`+`padding-bottom`) missed because the clip was the whole bottom **tray** pushed past the viewport, not the carousel. Surface = the shared stage-agnostic `CommandCentreShell` (Observe/Plan/Act); `.shell` grid (`auto minmax(0,1fr) auto`) is the sole direct child of AppShell's `.main` (`flex:1; position:relative; overflow:hidden`). **Root cause — two facts in `.shell` combined:** (1) `height:100%` didn't reliably bound the grid against the positioned `.main`, so it rendered auto-height and the `1fr` body row stretched to the **tallest column** (Act's tall right ops rail), pushing the `auto` tray row below the viewport where `.main{overflow:hidden}` clipped the cards — worst on All Modules/Tracker (tallest rail; the carousel is horizontal, so item count *widens* not *heightens*). (2) No explicit grid **column** → implicit `auto` column grew to the widest row's max-content (long carousel/tab strip), ballooning the body to ~9710px and shoving the rail off-screen (latent horizontal blowout). **Fix (CSS-only, `.shell`):** `height:100%`→`position:absolute; inset:0` (definite height → grid clamps, sidebar/rail scroll internally, tray always visible) + add `grid-template-columns: minmax(0,1fr)` (pins rows to viewport width; inner `overflow:auto` scrolls within its box). One shared sheet fixes all three stages uniformly; purely presentational (no JSX/store/schema/model/migration — covenant-clean). **Verified:** live DOM (`preview_eval`) shell bounded 812px (=`.main` height), body 1416 with sidebar 268/map 784/rail 340 all on-screen (`railOnScreen:true`, `trayWithinViewport:true`) **+ a confirming screenshot** of the full Act layout incl. intact Tracker cards (per the preview-verification rule — captured, not assumed); checked the failing All Modules/Tracker tabs + a low-count tab (no regression). **Process:** an early `git add` swept 61 files (60 pre-existing foreign staged); recovered via `reset --soft HEAD~1` + unstage-all + explicit-path add (final = 1 file), prior index restored. Foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]]; explicit-path commit per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]] (commit survived a later out-of-band rebase [[project-branch-rebase]], reflog-confirmed; HEAD now `f5a4cd94`). ADR [[decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-command-centre-shell-bounding]]; continues [[log/2026-05-25-command-centre-tray-and-waterrouter-fixes]] + [[log/2026-05-25-observe-command-centre-dashboard-shell]].

- [2026-05-25 — Sync-queue circuit-breaker (propagate failures + surface drops)](log/2026-05-25-sync-circuit-breaker.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`84bb8e91`, 5 files +322/−37). Closed the circuit-breaker deferred by [[log/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-fix]]: `flush()`'s retry/backoff/drop machinery only engages when the executor **throws**, but `executeQueuedOp` routed create/update through the *swallowing* live-path handlers (`try { api } catch { warn; enqueue }`) — so a failing queued op never incremented `retryCount`, never backed off, and (after the coalescing-key fix) re-enqueued under the same key `flush()` just dequeued → **silently dropped after one pass**. Fix: a `rethrow = false` param on each swallowing create/update handler (`syncProject/Zone/Structure/Path/Utility Create/Update`, `syncProjectBoundary`, generic `typedCreate`/`typedUpdate`) re-throws before the re-enqueue; `executeQueuedOp` create/update now pass `true` (delete/state-blob/comment already throw). New `handleExhaustedOp` wired as `flush()`'s new `onDrop` callback → records the dropped key in a new `droppedStores` channel on `connectivityStore` (dedupe, not persisted) + one `toast.error`; `OfflineBanner` gets a new highest-severity "could not be saved — kept on this device" banner with dismissable chips. Live path unchanged (default `rethrow=false`). Verified: typecheck exit 0; new `syncServiceCircuitBreaker.test.ts` (6) + 123 existing sync tests green. **Phase 2 static audit:** the dormant full-coverage path behind `FLAGS.SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` (off by default) is fully wired + unit-verified (129/129) — classification/guard, flag-gated push+pull, 409 never-clobber, version-skew guard; flagged `ogden-projects` double-classification (`active-singleton`/`whole` **and** typed `subscribeToProjects`) for the E2E. Deferred (human-gated): two-device E2E + `FEATURE_SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` rollout; `projectBundle.ts` kept (no-deletion). The drop-surfacing is the safety property that makes rollout safe. ADR [[decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-sync-circuit-breaker]]; hardens [[concepts/local-first-architecture]] ahead of [[concepts/full-syncservice-coverage-backlog]].
- [2026-05-25 — Sync-queue OOM fix (coalescing key + bounded flush)](log/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-fix.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`e5e8f220`). Fixed recurring Chrome "Out of Memory" crash on command-centre routes. Root cause (confirmed via a "Syncing 254520 changes…" screenshot, after refuting every in-render hypothesis by measurement): the IndexedDB sync queue was an unbounded append log — `enqueue()` keyed ops by random UUID so the same failing entity re-queued forever, and `flush()` loaded the whole queue via `getAll()` (250k ops × GeoJSON = multi-GB) into the JS heap. Fix: coalescing deterministic key `storeType:action:localId` (re-queue overwrites → growth bounded), `getBatch(limit)` cursor read + `FLUSH_BATCH=200` instead of `getAll()`, `reconcile()` one-time cursor collapse run at `syncService.start()`, and `flush()` now drops exhausted ops. Verified: 20k-op runaway reconciled to 5 with heap flat ~71–74 MB then drained to 0; typecheck exit 0. Deferred: circuit-breaker for the ~14 swallow-and-re-enqueue executor handlers. ADR [[decisions/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix]]; hardens [[concepts/local-first-architecture]].

Closes the deferred guard item from [[log/2026-05-25-fix-olos-login-failed-to-fetch]]: an unreachable backend (API down / dead origin / stale offline-PWA shell) rendered the raw browser `TypeError: Failed to fetch` on the login form. A network-level fetch rejection is re-thrown **unchanged** from `apiClient.request()` (`apps/web/src/lib/apiClient.ts:156-170`) — a deliberate contract asserted by `apiClient.clientError.test.ts:59-69` and relied on by stores that fall back to local data (`projectStore`, `ArchivePage`, `commentStore`, `memberStore`). **Fix placed at the auth boundary, not in apiClient** (central wrapping would break that contract): new `authErrorMessage(err, fallback)` in `authStore.ts` used by `login()`+`register()` — `ApiError`→server message verbatim (401 "Invalid email or password" etc.), `TypeError`→branch on `navigator.onLine` (offline → "You appear to be offline…"; online-but-unreachable, the real dead-origin case → "Can't reach the server. It may be offline or still starting up — try reloading…"). `LoginPage.tsx` unchanged (renders `{error}` verbatim). `reportApiFailure` telemetry (`NETWORK_ERROR`/`status:0`) unaffected. **Verified:** new `authStore.networkError.test.ts` (4 cases) + existing apiClient contract = **14/14**; my files `tsc`-clean (3 pre-existing foreign-WIP test errors untouched); live :5200 fetch-stub → `role="alert"` shows the friendly message (`preview_screenshot` times out on WebGL — accessibility-tree text read, **stated not claimed**). - [2026-05-25 — fix(ops): OLOS login "Failed to fetch" — API down + DB behind](log/2026-05-25-fix-olos-login-failed-to-fetch.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Operational fix, **no source changes**. Login showed `TypeError: Failed to fetch`; root cause = the Fastify **API was not running on 3001** (`ECONNREFUSED`), so the Vite proxy (`/api` → `localhost:3001`) had nothing to forward to. Raw "Failed to fetch" (not the proxy's friendly `503 API_OFFLINE`) because the browser tab was on a **dead origin** — standard web port 5200 was also down (only a `web-5201` parallel session was live); a no-response fetch makes `apiClient` re-throw the raw error (`apps/web/src/lib/apiClient.ts:156-170`). **Red herring:** `docker exec ogden-postgres psql` showed the DB at migration 037 while `pnpm migrate` (over `DATABASE_URL`→`localhost:5432`) showed 042 — because a **native `postgresql-x64-17` Windows service** owns `localhost:5432` (the DB the API uses) and the docker `ogden-postgres` container is stale + shadowed; documented in [[entities/database]] (always check DB state over TCP, never `docker exec`). **Fix:** applied pending migrations (`042_fix_farm_project_type` clean), started API (clean boot, PG+Redis connected, `/health` 200), started web on 5200. **Verified:** in-browser `fetch('/api/v1/auth/login')` with bad creds → real `401 UNAUTHORIZED "Invalid email or password"` (no more "Failed to fetch"). The proxy's `API_OFFLINE` 503 only protects users on a *live* origin; a stale tab / offline-PWA cache (`FEATURE_OFFLINE=true`) on a dead origin still shows raw "Failed to fetch" — flagged, not changed.

- [2026-05-25 — Blob-sync ramp Stage 1: real-Postgres validation surfaces two flip-blocking bugs](log/2026-05-25-blobsync-stage1-validation-two-latent-bugs.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`, commit `e6b48857` (2 files, +20/−4). First run of `blobSync.integration` (cases A/B/C) against a **live Postgres** for Stage 1 of the `FLAGS.SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` ramp — caught two latent `/project-state` route bugs the FIFO-mock suites cannot see. **(1)** `rev` (`BIGINT`) comes back from postgres.js as a **string**, failing `ProjectStateBlob.parse` (`z.number`) → **422 on every successful PUT**; coerced in `parseRow`. **(2)** the PUT pre-stringified then cast `::jsonb`, **double-encoding** the payload into a jsonb string scalar (`jsonb_typeof = string`); the client does no `JSON.parse` so hydration would load stores with a string — fixed with `${db.json(...)}::jsonb` (serialize once). - [2026-05-25 — Compass toast reads real How-checks, not seed evidence](log/2026-05-25-compass-toast-reads-real-checks.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`73ff75a0`, 3 files). See ADR [[2026-05-25-atlas-compass-toast-reads-real-checks]]. Steward screenshot bug: the Observe **HUMAN CONTEXT** panel read **"33% · 1/3 steps"** (only the last How checkbox ticked) yet the in-map **"Objective complete"** toast fired — "Just because the last task on the list is marked complete it renders the whole objective as complete." Chose to fix **all three stages** (AskUserQuestion). **Root cause:** two parallel progress systems read different sources — the visible panel (`GuidanceCard` via `*ChecklistAside`) uses `progressFromChecks(checked, how.length)` over the **real** per-stage How-checks store (→1/3 ✓), but the toast (`*ObjectiveCompletePrompt` via the single-objective hooks `use*ObjectiveProgress`) used `objectiveProgress` over the **seed-backed compass** store, where `isVerified = raw[i]==='verified' || checked.includes(i)`; the Observe `human-context` SEED `{0:'verified',1:'verified',2:'evidence-in'}` + the one real tick on node 2 = 3/3 = 100% → false toast. Purely SEED-as-completion, not a count mismatch (`nodes.length === how.length` since compass nodes are `how.map(...)`). **Fix (3 files, −12 net):** repoint each single-objective hook (`useCompassData.ts`/`usePlanCompassData.ts`/`useActCompassData.ts`) to `progressFromChecks(checks ?? EMPTY_CHECKS, obj.nodes.length)`, dropping the `seedFor` evidence read + `evidence` dep; compass-store imports stay (the plural `use*CompassData` **wheel** hook still uses SEED for its prototype). Toast components unchanged (their `pct===100` gate is correct once fed real numbers). **Verified in-browser** (:5200): Observe 1/3→no toast (screenshot), 3/3→toast (screenshot), untick→toast gone; Plan `livestock` 2/4→no toast, 4/4→toast; Act `tracker` seed-gap analog (SEED verifies 0+1) driven via localStorage — node-2-only→no toast, 3/3→toast (screenshot), test state cleaned up. `objectiveStatus.test.ts` 10/10; `tsc` clean for the 3 files (only the **known 3-error foreign-WIP baseline** remains — `StepBoundary.tsx`, two `HostUnion*` tests; `tsc` OOMs at default heap, re-ran with `--max-old-space-size=8192`). Staged by **explicit path** per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]], foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]], divergence-checked (1 ahead/0 behind) before push.

- [2026-05-25 — Compass progress fill: outside-in (rim → centre)](log/2026-05-25-compass-progress-fill-outside-in.md) — **Branch.** atlas `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`d181f223`, 2 files) + `ogden-ui-components` `release/v0.1.1`/tag `v0.1.1` (`e71fcc3`). Steward, looking at the **True North** compass, asked each progress wedge to **fill from the outer rim inward toward the hub** as completion rises (full wedge at 100%, sliver at the rim near 0%), reversing the prior centre→rim fill. **The non-obvious part: the wheel isn't in atlas.** It's the shared `MaqasidComparisonWheel` in the separate repo `@ogden/ui-components`, consumed as a **pinned GitHub tarball** whose `dist/` is **committed** — so the fix is a cross-repo release: edit source + rebuild/commit `dist/` in the component repo, then bump atlas's pin. **Steward decisions (AskUserQuestion):** (a) **surgical patch v0.1.1** off the `v0.1.0` tag (avoids pulling intervening additive BBOS/educational components into atlas); (b) **all wheels** — flip once in the shared component, no opt-in prop. **The change = 3 lines, one file:** the existing `annularSector(rInner, rOuter,…)` helper already takes both radii, so progress flips from a *moving outer* radius (`currentR = HUB_R + (PROGRESS_MAX_R-HUB_R)·pct`) to a *moving inner* radius (`fillInnerR = PROGRESS_MAX_R - (PROGRESS_MAX_R-HUB_R)·pct`; `HUB_R=56`, `PROGRESS_MAX_R=142`), with the `mcw-seg-current` fill + `mcw-seg-pattern` overlay drawn as `annularSector(fillInnerR, PROGRESS_MAX_R,…)`. Dim track / 0%-empty ring / complete-arc / gradient / entrance animation untouched — **no CSS change**. **Blast radius = 5 atlas surfaces** (True North, Observe, Plan, Act, OPA dashboard wheel); the separate `CycleWheel` is out of scope. **Release+pin:** branched from `v0.1.0`, `npm run build` regenerated dist, committed source+dist (`e71fcc3`), tagged+pushed; atlas pin `#v0.1.0`→`#v0.1.1` (root `package.json` only; `apps/web` doesn't pin), `corepack pnpm install` → lockfile resolves `e71fcc3`. **Verification:** `preview_screenshot` times out (MapLibre/WebGL, **stated not claimed**); verified by a deterministic geometry probe of the **installed** minified bundle — fill resolves to `a = H - (H - B)·(i/100)` with `H=142`/`B=56` and the path call `annularSector(a, H,…)`, i.e. outer pinned at 142, inner tracks pct (142 at 0% → 56 at 100%); conclusive since geometry is a pure fn of pct. Atlas staged by **explicit path** (`package.json`+`pnpm-lock.yaml`), foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]], divergence-checked before push per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]. **Addendum — "wheel looks unchanged" root cause + forward-port:** the steward then reported the wheel looked the same; investigation found the code was correct but the app **served stale pixels** — (1) the **v0.1.1 release never bumped `package.json` `version`** (stuck at `0.1.0`), so caches had no invalidation signal *(the real defect)*, and (2) atlas's `optimizeDeps.exclude` serves the dep raw and vite **doesn't watch `node_modules`**, so the dev server running since before the install kept its old transform. **Fix:** restart the dev server + clear `apps/web/node_modules/.vite`; DOM-probe then confirmed outer arc fixed at 142 / inner tracks pct = rim→centre (`preview_screenshot` times out on WebGL, stated not claimed). **Lesson:** *a release must bump `package.json` `version`, not just move a tag.* **Forward-port done:** same 3-line flip applied to `ogden-ui-components` `main`, `version` bumped 0.3.0→**0.3.1** (defect not repeated), dist rebuilt (diff limited to the `index` bundles + maps), committed by explicit path, **tagged `v0.3.1`**, pushed (`46a1815..90aa7c6`). v0.1.1 left intact; atlas pin-to-v0.3.1 noted as non-blocking follow-up. **Addendum — atlas pin bumped v0.1.1 → v0.3.1 (`77fe24af`):** closed that follow-up — pin `#v0.1.1`→`#v0.3.1` so atlas now carries the **correct `version` field** (0.3.1), closing the cache-busting defect; same wheel geometry, plus additive BBOS/educational (zero bundle impact — atlas imports only the wheel/hover-store/LevelNavigator, BBOS is a separate dist entry). **The gotcha:** v0.3.x changed the dist from single-file (`dist/ogden-ui-components.es.js`) to **multi-entry** (`dist/index.es.js` + `dist/bbos.es.js`), and atlas resolves via a hardcoded **vite alias** (not the `exports` map), so the alias was repointed `dist/ogden-ui-components.es.js`→`dist/index.es.js` (CSS alias unchanged — same filename). **Verified:** installed `version` = 0.3.1; `dist/index.es.js` carries `a = H - (H - V)·(i/100)` drawn `ue(a,H,…)`; live wheel DOM-probe outer-fixed-142/inner-tracks-pct (rim→centre); `vite build` resolves the repointed alias in 39.5s (the `tsc && vite build` script's `tsc` step fails on the known 3-error foreign-WIP baseline — ran `vite build` directly). Explicit-path commit (`package.json`+`apps/web/vite.config.ts`+`pnpm-lock.yaml`), foreign WIP untouched, divergence-checked. Plan: `~/.claude/plans/light-mode-of-the-splendid-crayon.md` (Parts 4–6).

- [2026-05-24 — MapLibre marker hover fix + temporary Command Centre unlock](log/2026-05-24-marker-hover-fix-and-command-centre-unlock.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Two small compass/map touch-ups. **(1) Bug fix `80f2b9d3`:** hovering a Command Centre objective marker made it jump to the map's top-left corner. Root cause — MapLibre writes the *entire* positioning `transform` (`translate(-50%,-50%) translate(x,y)…`) onto a DOM marker's own element each frame; the `mouseenter` handler set `el.style.transform = 'scale(...)'` on that **same** element, erasing the translate → marker snapped to the container origin until the next position write. Fix: move the hover scale to an inner `pin` child (`line-height:0` outer shrink-wraps it; geometry unchanged, clicks bubble); fixed in both `ObjectiveMapMarkers.tsx` (reported) and `FieldFlagOverlay.tsx` (identical pattern). Other DOM-marker overlays don't hover-transform (grep-verified). **Reusable lesson: never write `transform` on a MapLibre marker element — scale an inner child.** **(2) Temp unlock `e615c6da`:** steward asked to enter the Observe Command Centre without all objectives verified; the center-unlock gate ([[decisions/2026-05-24-atlas-observe-command-centre]]) is one `ready` flag in `StageCompassPage.tsx` driving the wheel hotspot's clickability + `forceConverged` glow + `onEnter()`. Forced `ready = data.views.length > 0`, marked **TEMP** with the exact one-line revert in a comment. Both pure presentation/behaviour — covenant clean, no schema/store/model/migration. `tsc` at the 3-error pre-existing baseline; committed by name per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]; live preview not run (MapLibre canvas hangs screenshots — documented standard).

- [2026-05-22 — Plan/Observe follow-ups: maplibre line-width fix + URL-persist picked section](log/2026-05-22-plan-observe-followups-linewidth-url-persist.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closed the two deferred follow-ups from [[log/2026-05-22-cross-rail-single-section-highlight]] (`fc0938b8`). **Part 1 — `design-el-line` line-width** (`apps/web/src/v3/plan/canvas/layers/DesignElementLayers.tsx`): the layer threw `paint.line-width: Only one zoom-based "step" or "interpolate" subexpression may be used` **every frame**, because a zoom-based `lineWidthExpr` was nested inside a `case` **and** referenced twice (`['case', selFlag, ['+', lineWidthExpr, 2], lineWidthExpr]`) — two nested zoom curves. MapLibre requires the zoom curve to be the **outermost** expression of a paint property (only the *input* must be `['zoom']`; feature-state is allowed in stop *outputs*). Fix: collapsed to a **single top-level** zoom `interpolate` with the `selFlag` `+2px` selection delta folded into each stop output; dropped the `case` wrap. Console buffer now clean of the error. **Part 2 — URL-persist `?section=`** (`PlanLayout.tsx` + `ObserveLayout.tsx`): moved `activeSectionId` from per-Layout `useState` to a URL **search param** (`useSearch({ strict:false }) as { section?: string }`), so the single-section cross-rail highlight survives reloads/back-forward/shared links. **No `validateSearch`** added — matches the `ObserveDeepLinkFocus` convention and avoids stripping the existing `focus*` deep-link params. Navigation collapsed into one `navigateModuleSection(mod, sectionId)` primitive writing the `$module` path + `?section` atomically (`navigate`'s `search` *replaces*, so passed explicitly every time); `handleSelectModule`→`(mod,null)` (whole family), `handleSelectSection` toggles on strict identity; PlanLayout's silvopasture-drilldown effect navigate also got `search:{}`. The four rail components are unchanged (already consume `effectiveSectionId`+`onSelectSection`). **Verification:** `cd apps/web && npm run typecheck` at the **3-error pre-existing baseline** (`StepBoundary.tsx`, two `HostUnion*` tests); live DOM/URL evals (:5200) — Plan cold-load `?section=be-agricultural`→2 active (survives reload), click narrows+writes `?section`, click active deselects+drops module&section (0), no-section→family (10); Observe `?section=be-building`→2, `be-from-map`→1 (main rail only, documented), no-section→family (13), live click writes `?section`. **Screenshot blocker root-cause corrected:** the prior session blamed the line-width error for the `preview_screenshot` 30 s timeout — **wrong.** With the error gone the screenshot still times out because the preview tab is **backgrounded** (`document.visibilityState==='hidden'`, `hasFocus()===false`), which throttles `requestAnimationFrame` so any frame-dependent op hangs while synchronous evals return instantly; `preview_resize` didn't foreground it. So the blocker is an **environment** condition (preview pane not focused), not renderer saturation and not the line-width bug — stated not assumed per the preview-verification rule; synchronous DOM/URL evals are authoritative here. Staged only the 3 files by explicit path; foreign WIP (EconomicsPanel, capitalPartner, SectorCompassOverlay, ZoneSomSidebar) untouched per `feedback_no_deletion`. Plan: `~/.claude/plans/the-sector-compass-in-memoized-sphinx.md`.

- [2026-05-22 — Cross-rail single-section highlight (Observe + both mini rails)](log/2026-05-22-cross-rail-single-section-highlight.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Generalizes the committed Plan-main-rail fix (`97182e38`, the "Plan rail single-section highlight" entry below) to **full cross-rail parity** with the steward-chosen **shared cross-rail state**: a section pick in the main rail propagates into the mini rail and vice-versa, so a stage shows exactly **one** active section everywhere (no "family-lit on arrival"). Before this, three rails still multi-lit — the **Observe main rail** (`ObserveTools`, three section families all routing to `built-environment`, lighting up to 7), and **both mini rails** (`PlanChecklistAside` / `ObserveChecklistAside`, `GuidanceCard`s keyed on `activeModule === routed`, so every BE card sharing a module lit together; Plan also has the machinery 2-way + structures-subsystems 5-way fan-out). **Approach: lift the section discriminator into each Layout** (mirroring the existing `slideUpOpen` lift), not a new store and no route-schema change. Each `*Layout` owns `activeSectionId: useState<string|null>` reconciled **lazily at render** into `effectiveSectionId = activeSectionId && sectionIdModule(activeSectionId) === validModule ? activeSectionId : null` (a stale id from reload / bottom-bar nav / deselect / the pre-navigate transient routes to a different module → ignored, so no race-prone `useEffect`). Three handlers split the former one: `navigateModule` (pure nav), `handleSelectModule` (`setActiveSectionId(null)` + nav — bottom bar / programmatic, clears narrow → whole family), `handleSelectSection` (toggle on strict identity — narrow/switch/deselect). Both `effectiveSectionId` + `onSelectSection` thread to **both** rails. **Uniform `isActive` in all four rails:** `effectiveSectionId !== null ? effectiveSectionId === sectionId : activeModule === routed` (`=== mod` for module sections); section ids reuse each section's React `key` (`mod`, `be-${category}`, `be-from-map`). **8 files:** 2 **new** centralized section maps (`plan/planSectionMap.ts`, `observe/observeSectionMap.ts` — each moves the formerly-duplicated `BE_CATEGORY_TO_*_MODULE` out of two rail files + adds a `*SectionIdModule(id)` helper; Observe's special-cases `be-from-map` **before** the be-slice) + 6 edited rail/Layout files (`PlanLayout`, `ObserveLayout`, `PlanTools`, `ObserveTools`, `PlanChecklistAside`, `ObserveChecklistAside`). **`GuidanceCard.tsx` unchanged** — its `onSelect` already fires only on inactive cards, exactly right under shared state. **Documented accepted behavior:** Observe "From map" sets `effectiveSectionId='be-from-map'` which matches no mini-rail card → mini rail shows **no** active card for that pick (it's a generic adopt meta-tool, not a BE category); a **cold URL load** with no prior click → family fallback (URL-persist is out of scope). **Verification:** `cd apps/web && npm run typecheck` at the **3-error pre-existing baseline** (`StepBoundary.tsx`, two `HostUnion*` tests), none in the 8 files; live DOM (Claude Preview :5200) `.groupActive` counts — Plan Agricultural→2, Buildings→2 (switch), active again→0 (deselect), Water Management (non-shared)→2, bottom-bar Structures→family 10; machinery module-level vs `be-machinery` each light alone; Observe Buildings→2, From map→1 (main only, documented), human-context→2. **Screenshot blocked by a pre-existing unrelated maplibre bug** (`DesignElementLayers.tsx` emits `paint.line-width: Only one zoom-based "step" or "interpolate" subexpression may be used` every frame, saturating the renderer → `preview_screenshot` 30 s timeout) — **not introduced here**; stated not assumed per the preview-verification rule, DOM counts authoritative. Staged only the 8 files by explicit path; concurrent-session foreign WIP untouched per `feedback_no_deletion`. Plan: `~/.claude/plans/the-sector-compass-in-memoized-sphinx.md`.

- 2026-05-22 — Plan rail single-section highlight (multi-highlight quirk fixed) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Follow-up to the Plan-rail-colors entry below: activating one Built-Environment category in the Plan left tool rail (`PlanTools`) lit **all** sections sharing its routed module, because `.groupActive` was decided solely by `activeModule === <routed module>` and five BE categories (building/agricultural/utility/infrastructure/amenity) route to `structures-subsystems` via `BE_CATEGORY_TO_PLAN_MODULE`. **Single-file change to `apps/web/src/v3/plan/PlanTools.tsx`** adds a local picked-section discriminator: `activeSectionId` (reuses each section's existing React `key` — `be-<category>` for BE sections, the module id for module sections), reconciled **lazily at render** into `effectiveId = activeSectionId && sectionIdModule(activeSectionId) === activeModule ? activeSectionId : null` — a stale id (reload, bottom-bar activation, deselect, or the brief transient before the async URL navigation resolves) is ignored, so no race-prone `useEffect`. The two `isActive` computations become `effectiveId === null ? activeModule === <routed> : effectiveId === <sectionId>`: when a section was explicitly picked only it lights; with no pick (reload / external nav) it falls back to today's whole-family highlight (documented no-regression). `onSectionActivate(mod, sectionId)` toggles on the strict identity so a family-lit section **narrows** to the clicked card rather than deselecting. **Verification (live, Claude Preview, scoped to the PlanTools rail `_group_duyuu_`):** `npm run typecheck` exit 0 at the 3-error pre-existing baseline (`StepBoundary.tsx`, two `HostUnion` tests); click Agricultural → exactly one `.groupActive`, **stable across 150 ms→4 s** (confirms PlanTools does not remount, so local state survives the async route commit); Buildings → highlight moves; Buildings again → deselects; standalone Machinery & Equipment and Water Management each light alone; direct load of `/structures-subsystems` lights the five BE cards as a family fallback, then a click narrows to one. Active styling confirmed via computed style (utility dot `rgb(106,166,217)`=`#6aa6d9`, active border + `aria-pressed`); screenshot tool unresponsive (timed out twice — stated, not assumed). **Concurrent-session change excluded from this commit:** the same file carried an unrelated machinery-fold (`beCategoryToolItems` helper + machinery `TOOL_GROUPS` spread + `if (group.category === 'machinery') return null;`) authored by a parallel session; staged only my multi-highlight hunks (backup/Edit/restore surgery), leaving the fold uncommitted for its owner. **Out of scope / follow-up:** the module-detail right panel renders its own mini rail (different CSS module `_group_1mx5x_`, `data-module='be-<category>'`) with the same latent multi-highlight; and the Observe rail (`ObserveTools`) where all six BE categories route to `built-environment` — both candidates for the same `effectiveId` pattern. - 2026-05-22 — Built-Environment rail groups get distinct accent colors (Plan — parity with Observe) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Follow-up to the prior Observe-rail entry below; the steward asked to bring the **Plan** stage rail to parity. Same `--group-dot` accent system, but the latent state **differed** from Observe's: Plan routes each BE category to a real Plan module via `BE_CATEGORY_TO_PLAN_MODULE` (`PlanTools.tsx:112-124`), and five of them (`building`, `agricultural`, `utility`, `infrastructure`, `amenity`) route to `structures-subsystems`, which **has** a color (`PlanTools.module.css:77`, terracotta-brown `#a06b48`) — so those five all shared one brown — while `machinery` routes to the rule-less `machinery` module and fell to the grey `--color-text-muted` default. **Pure-CSS, single-file, additive** change to `apps/web/src/v3/plan/PlanTools.module.css` — six `data-be-category` overrides added **after** the per-module block (line 83) using the **exact same hexes as Observe** (building `#c08457`, agricultural `#d9a45b`, utility `#6aa6d9`, infrastructure `#9a8bd6`, machinery `#c0705e`, amenity `#46b39d`). Specificity: each BE `<section>` carries both `data-module` and `data-be-category` (equal one-class+one-attribute specificity), so the category rules win by source order (declared after the module rules) — beating both the `structures-subsystems` brown and the grey default. **Observe's slate `data-module='built-environment'` base rule was deliberately omitted** — Plan has no "From map" meta-section, so it would be dead code. No markup/TSX change (`PlanTools.tsx:656-661` already emits both attributes; every visual element derives from `--group-dot`). **Verification (live, both rails):** `npm run typecheck` at the 3-error pre-existing baseline (CSS-only, no new errors); via Claude Preview computed-style inspection, all six BE dots in the **Plan** rail return the exact target RGBs (e.g. agricultural `rgb(217,164,91)`=`#d9a45b`, machinery `rgb(192,112,94)`=`#c0705e`), and the **Observe** rail returns the identical six values — confirming parity. One Plan-stage screenshot captured; the scroll-to-BE-groups screenshot timed out (tool unresponsive, stated not assumed), but the per-element computed colors are the authoritative confirmation. **Pre-existing quirk noted (out of scope):** because five BE categories route to one `structures-subsystems` module, activating one may mark all five `.groupActive` simultaneously — unaffected by this color change. Plan: `~/.claude/plans/the-sector-compass-in-memoized-sphinx.md`.

- [2026-05-22 — Client-error telemetry: `api_client` source wired (sink complete)](log/2026-05-22-client-error-telemetry-api-client-source.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Commit `004e4ad7`. Closes the last gap from [the sources-wired session](log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sources-wired.md): the `client_error_events` sink has **four** `source` values and the fourth, **`api_client`**, was still dark — API failures surfaced only as thrown `ApiError`s + uncaught network rejections, invisible server-side. **Scope (operator-confirmed):** report **all** failures (every `ApiError` incl. 401, **and** network/offline `fetch` rejections as `status:0`/`code:'NETWORK_ERROR'`, re-thrown unchanged); always-on **loop guard** excludes `/api/v1/telemetry/*` so a failed client-errors POST can't report itself; deliberate `AbortError`s skipped. **`apiClient.ts`** gains reporter-injection plumbing mirroring `setSessionExpiredHandler` (`ApiClientErrorReport` + `setApiClientErrorReporter` + private `reportApiFailure`); `request()` now wraps `fetch` in try/catch (reports non-abort rejections, re-throws original) and reports at the `ApiError` throw site before throwing. **Bundle-split preserved** — apiClient does **not** import `clientErrorLog` (would cycle, since clientErrorLog imports `api`, and drag the buffer into always-mounted code per [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]]); instead **`bootAuthed.ts`** (authed-only) registers the bridge `setApiClientErrorReporter((r) => recordClientError({ source:'api_client', ... }))`, `projectId` omitted so the active-project resolver stamps it. `stack`/`details` deliberately omitted (uninformative / payload-lean / no body leak). **Tests:** new `apiClient.clientError.test.ts` (happy-dom, stubbed `fetch`, spy reporter) — 6/6 green (5xx reported, 401 reported, network reported+rethrown, AbortError not reported, loop guard, no-reporter safe); web tsc shows only the 3 pre-existing unrelated baseline errors. **Follow-up (same day, commits `82d2bb19` code + `0f86be26` wiki):** the two upload throw sites are now wired too — `files.upload` (XHR) gains a `fail()` helper reporting each `ApiError` reject site (non-2xx `onload`, parse `catch`, `onerror`), and `regenerationEvents.uploadMedia` (fetch) became `async` with the same try/catch-around-fetch + report-before-throw pattern as `request()`; 4 new test cases (XHR stub + fetch mock) → 10/10 green, tsc baseline unchanged. **Every API failure path now emits `api_client` telemetry — no dark paths remain.** ADR back-links: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]], [[log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sources-wired]].
