- [2026-05-21 — Client-error telemetry: react_error_boundary + unhandled_rejection wired, migration 039 applied](log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sources-wired.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Direct follow-up to [the client-error telemetry sink](log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sink.md), which shipped `recordClientError` + the buffered POST pipeline + the `client_error_events` table but left three of its four `source` enum values unused. This session wires the **two highest-value remaining sources** and applies the table migration. **`react_error_boundary`** — both error boundaries in `apps/web/src/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx` (generic `ErrorBoundary` + always-mounted `GlobalErrorBoundary`) now call a shared `reportBoundaryError(error, info, boundary)` from `componentDidCatch`, emitting `source:'react_error_boundary'` with `context.boundary` + a 4000-char-capped `componentStack`. Because `GlobalErrorBoundary` mounts on every path incl. `/showcase/*`, the helper uses a **lazy `import('../lib/clientErrorLog.js')`** to keep the authed graph out of the showcase initial chunk ([[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]]). **`unhandled_rejection`** — new `apps/web/src/lib/globalErrorHandlers.ts` (`installGlobalErrorHandlers()`) registers one idempotent `window.unhandledrejection` listener; it statically imports `clientErrorLog`, so it is imported **only from `bootAuthed.ts`** (authed-only — showcase ships no client-error telemetry). `window.onerror` deliberately out of scope (no matching enum source; React render errors already covered). **projectId resolver** — `clientErrorLog.ts` gains `setClientErrorProjectIdResolver(fn)`; `recordClientError` uses `input.projectId !== undefined ? input.projectId : safeResolveProjectId()` so an explicit value (incl. the persist helper's explicit `null`) wins, an omitted one falls back to the resolver (`bootAuthed.ts` registers `() => useProjectStore.getState().activeProjectId ?? null`); `safeResolveProjectId` swallows resolver throws. **Migration 039 applied to the LOCAL DEV DB** — investigation confirmed there is **no prod/staging DB** (staging parked, [[log/2026-04-21-staging-provisioning-decision-parked]]); only local dev Postgres exists, operator confirmed. Runner applies all pending in order (can't target one), so 039 + additive 040/041 (`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS`, verified non-destructive) applied together via `node --env-file=.env --import=tsx src/db/migrate.ts`. Verified `client_error_events`: 14 cols, nullable `project_id`/`stack`, 2 indexes, 4-source CHECK constraint; `039` in `schema_migrations`. **Tests:** new `globalErrorHandlers.test.ts` (3) + `ErrorBoundary.telemetry.test.tsx` (3) + extended `clientErrorLog.test.ts` resolver block (3) — 20 targeted tests green; web tsc shows only the 3 pre-existing unrelated errors. Commit `2eb2aa6a` (frontend slice). **Remaining gap:** `api_client` is the last unwired source (deferred — lower value). ADR back-links: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]], [[log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sink]].
- [2026-05-21 — Phase 5 (Slice B): Showcase observation loop](log/2026-05-21-atlas-phase-5-observation.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. The final phase of the Apricot-Lane-inspired Showcase Program — adds the observation loop the public `/showcase/three-streams` portal ([[log/2026-05-21-atlas-phase-3-showcase-portal]]) shipped without. Two blockers: the authed telemetry pipeline (`POST /api/v1/telemetry/act-interactions` + `act_interaction_events`) is `authenticate`-gated and its `user_id`/`project_id` are both NOT NULL — a cold showcase visitor is anonymous by definition. **Decision: a parallel anonymous-first path, not a relaxed authed one** ([[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-observation-loop]]); the authed pipeline is left untouched. **Quantitative half** — migration `040_showcase_visitor_events.sql` (`bb54a4fb`) inverts the NOT-NULL invariants (nullable `user_id`/`project_id`; `session_id` the cross-event handle; `event_type` CHECK on 7 lifecycle events; `tier` CHECK NULL-or-enum; idempotent) + PUBLIC rate-limited (`60/min`) `POST /api/v1/telemetry/showcase-events` with best-effort `jwtVerify` (stamps `user_id` only if a bearer happens to be present) and best-effort per-event bulk insert (`cbe90535`). **Client wiring** (`57de13f8`) — `showcaseEventLog.ts` mirrors `actInteractionLog.ts`'s batcher shape but POSTs via plain `fetch` + `navigator.sendBeacon` with type-only `@ogden/shared` imports (keeps the Phase 3.5 lean SSG bundle free of `authStore`/`projectStore`/Cesium); instruments `TierChooser`/`ContactCTA`/route-mount/register/instantiate. **Qualitative half** — migration `041_showcase_feedback.sql` + PUBLIC `POST /api/v1/telemetry/showcase-feedback` + `FeedbackForm.tsx` mounted between `<ContactCTA>` and `<AttributionFooter>` (`051518e9`); `message` the one required field (client + route trim + DB CHECK backstop), `rating`/`contact` opt-in, reads (not creates) the telemetry `session_id` to cross-link, deliberately ungated by `VITE_ATLAS_TELEMETRY_ENABLED` (explicit submission is opt-in, not passive telemetry). **Covenant ratchet** (`f3a5aeb8`) — `covenant.test.ts`'s `git ls-files` subtree scan pulled both new files in scope automatically; one catch-and-fix where the `FeedbackForm` docstring *enumerated* the forbidden tokens and tripped the ratchet on its own prose (reworded). **Privacy posture:** anonymous by default (ephemeral `sessionStorage` id, no cookie/fingerprint/PII), the only PII channel (`showcase_feedback.contact`) is opt-in, cross-link not identity; consent banner deferred (documented in ADR). Gate: API tsc exit 0; web tsc 0 new errors above baseline; showcase vitest green incl. covenant ratchet + Apricot Lane exact-string. **Program complete** (Phase 0 → 5). ADR back-links: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-observation-loop]], [[entities/showcase-portal]], [[log/2026-05-21-atlas-phase-2.5-livestock-seed]].

- [2026-05-21 — Phase G hotfix: Vite alias for `@ogden/shared/evidence`](log/2026-05-21-phase-g-vite-alias-hotfix.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Unblocks dev-server boot after Phase G G.1 added `./evidence` to `packages/shared/package.json` exports but did not update the parallel `resolve.alias` map in `apps/web/vite.config.ts`. Symptom: Vite v6.4.1 returned HTTP 500 on `DecisionTriad.tsx` / `LandVerdictCard.tsx` / `auditEmit.ts` with "Failed to resolve import `@ogden/shared/evidence`"; React root never mounted. Root cause: `vite.config.ts:172-196` carries an explicit alias map for every `@ogden/shared/*` subpath because Vite's dev-server cwd is `apps/web/` and cannot traverse up to the workspace-root node_modules; the bare `@ogden/shared` entry prefix-matched any unaliased subpath and rewrote it to `packages/shared/src/index.ts/evidence` (nonsense). Node's resolver was happy (verified via `require.resolve`); Vite's alias-first chain short-circuited before reaching the exports field. Fix: one-line add at `apps/web/vite.config.ts:194` — `'@ogden/shared/evidence': resolve(__dirname, '../../packages/shared/src/evidence/index.ts')` — placed before the bare-package fallback per the "more-specific first" rule in the surrounding comment. Verification: all three modules HTTP 200; `apps/web` typecheck clean for evidence code (3 pre-existing unrelated errors untouched: `StepBoundary.tsx`, `HostUnionContextMenu.test.tsx`, `HostUnionDrilldownCard.test.tsx`). Lesson: future subpath additions to `packages/shared/package.json` exports **must also** add the matching `vite.config.ts` alias entry — the two surfaces are parallel and Vite's prefix-match silently fails for any apps/web consumer otherwise.
- [2026-05-21 — Phase G: server-side evidence-audit replay tool](log/2026-05-21-phase-g-evidence-audit-replay.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. - [2026-05-21 — Click-delete vertex fix (onMouseUp → onClick)](log/2026-05-21-click-delete-vertex-fix.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Bug-fix for user-reported "clicking on a vertex does not remove it" in real Chrome. Root cause: `clickDeleteDirectSelect.ts` attached deletion to `onMouseUp`, but MapboxDraw's `events.mouseup` routes click-gestures (`isClick`: ≤ 4 px / ≤ 500 ms) to `currentMode.onClick`, drag-releases to `currentMode.onMouseUp` — so plain vertex clicks never reached the delete branch. Two slices: **`90fef60a`** moved deletion to `onClick`, dropped the now-redundant in-mode pixel-threshold (MapboxDraw's own `isClick` already gates), and returns early without delegating to `stock.onClick` when the min-vertex guard fires (otherwise `clickActiveFeature` clears `selectedCoordPaths` and kicks the user out of vertex-edit on the 3rd vertex of a triangle); also resets `_cdVertexCoordPath` on every `onMouseDown`. **`16dc2d79`** appended a corrective "later" section to the [partial smoke-walk log](log/2026-05-21-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete.md) striking through its "harness limitation" framing — the harness was a red herring layered on top of a real regression. Typecheck exit 0. Real-browser keystroke confirmation of the remaining smoke-walk steps still owed. Branch hygiene: stashed unrelated parallel-session edits (basemap-water-adoption + template_slug migration) before commit, restored after push; `git fetch` 2/0 before push; FF clean.

Mirrors the existing `AdoptBasemapBuildingTool` for the OpenMapTiles `water` + `waterway` source-layers. New `Waterbody` entity in [`waterSystemsStore`](../../apps/web/src/store/waterSystemsStore.ts) (polygon, kinds lake/pond/wetland/reservoir/other) alongside the existing `Watercourse`. - [2026-05-21 — Observe-anno "stuck source" diagnosis closed as headless-RAF artefact](log/2026-05-21-observe-anno-sources-false-alarm.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. **No code change.** Wiki-only documentation closing the "four observe-anno sources never reach `loaded:true`" investigation as not-a-bug. Live preview verification at `/v3/project/mtc/observe` with two seeded Conventional Crop polygons shows `m.isSourceLoaded('observe-anno-conventional-crop') === true` and `queryRenderedFeatures` returning the crop with correct `annoKind`/`annoId` props — after exactly one `_render()` tick. The prior session's "render loop is dead" conclusion was a property-name miss: it probed `m._frame`, but MapLibre 5.x renamed that field to `_frameRequest` and now schedules frames via `AbortController` + `browser.frameAsync` ([`node_modules/maplibre-gl/dist/maplibre-gl-dev.js:57944`](../node_modules/maplibre-gl/dist/maplibre-gl-dev.js)). Re-probing the correct field shows a frame IS queued — it just never resolves while the Claude Preview tab is backgrounded (headless Chrome throttles RAF for inactive tabs). All geojson sources show the same idle-paused profile in the preview (`be-v2-*`, `matrix-*-dem`, `design-el-extrusion`, `diagnose-parcel-boundary`), not just the named four; the "siblings load normally" framing in the brief was a probe-timing artefact. **Diagnostic technique worth keeping:** when debugging "isSourceLoaded never true" under Claude Preview, force a paint via `m._render(performance.now())` from the eval console to drain `_updatedSources` and resume paused SourceCaches synchronously enough to read a real state. **Implication for the [vertex-edit + click-delete smoke walk](log/2026-05-21-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete.md):** if "clicks don't open detail panels" reproduces in a real browser, the cause is not stuck sources — likelier suspects are `SelectionFloater` consuming the click before the layer handler, the 50 ms `consumedAt` deduper in `ObserveAnnotationLayers.tsx` mis-rejecting, or the form store's `existingId === id && kind === kind` early-return. Disposition: closed as not-a-bug; future sessions should re-test in a real browser before re-opening this thread.

- [2026-05-21 — Observe matrix+patches model + Fill-remainder tool](log/2026-05-21-observe-matrix-patches-and-fill-remainder.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Single commit `2a6def92`. Vegetation + pasture now describe the ground-cover *matrix*; crops + buildings sit on top as opaque *patches* rather than translucent blends. Four phases in one slice: (1) `conventionalCrop` fill-opacity 0.22 → 0.55 and `building` 0.35 → 0.6 in `ObserveAnnotationLayers.tsx` so patches occlude the matrix underneath (layer-order already correct). (2) New pure `netCoverAreaM2(patches, subtractees)` in `earth-water-ecology/derivations.ts` — per-patch `turf.area − Σ turf.area(turf.intersect(patch, sub))`, clamped at zero, summed; wired into `ecologyDetailKpis` with subtractees = crops ∪ buildings; surfaces as a new "Ground cover (net)" KPI in `EcologicalDetail`. 5 new vitest cases pin empty/no-subtractees/enclosed/fully-covered/non-overlapping. `@turf/turf` v7 trap noted: `turf.intersect` takes a `FeatureCollection` of two polygons, not two positional `Feature` args. (3) `vegetationStore` + `pastureStore` geometry widened to `GeoJSON.Polygon | GeoJSON.MultiPolygon` so Fill-remainder can store disjoint pieces; `annotationGeometryRegistry.writePolygon` accepts the union with per-kind narrowing (hazard/building/septic/conventionalCrop early-return on MultiPolygon, vegetation/pasture accept both); `readPolygon` returns the union; `annotationFieldSchemas` vegetation/pasture save guards widened. MapboxDraw `direct_select` only handles single Polygons, so `AnnotationVertexEditHandler.readPolygon` adapter narrows to Polygon-only (returns `null` for MultiPolygon) — vertex-edit gracefully disables on those records, drag-reposition still works. MapLibre fill/line layers handle MultiPolygon natively, no paint change. (4) New **"Fill remainder (subtract crops & buildings)"** checkbox in `VegetationTool` and `PastureTool` popovers — when on, `place(boundary)` runs `subtractPatches`: reduce `turf.difference(turf.featureCollection([acc, turf.feature(g)]))` over crops ∪ buildings; `null` result (boundary fully covered) bails with a `console.info` and skips creation, otherwise the Polygon/MultiPolygon flows through the existing `createWithDefaults() → form → addPatch()` path. No new store API beyond the Phase 3 schema bump. **Verification.** `npx --no-install vitest run` (full apps/web) 1703/1703 across 173 files (+5 over the prior 1698). `npm run lint` (= `tsc --noEmit`) clean. DOM check at `/v3/project/mtc/observe`: both popovers render the checkbox. Screenshot tool unresponsive (map-tile blocking the renderer); flagged transparently per CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success." **Out of scope.** Snap-to-existing-edge, render-time masking, crop/raised-bed MultiPolygon, Plan-stage changes, toast UI on full-coverage bail, vertex-edit on MultiPolygon (intentionally disabled), DB / shared-package schema changes. **Branch governance.** Fetched + verified no divergence prior to commit per [[project-branch-rebase]]; committed the moment lint + tests cleared per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]].

Silent refusal per user choice — no toast. `SharedVertexEditHandler.tsx` registers the mode on the per-mount `MapboxDraw` instance and switches `changeMode` from `'direct_select'` to `CLICK_DELETE_DIRECT_SELECT`; Plan-stage `PlanVertexEditHandler` inherits for free via composition. **Behaviour.** Click vertex (no drag) → vertex deleted; click+drag → moves (unchanged); midpoint click → adds vertex (unchanged); click vertex on triangle / 2-vertex line → nothing (silently gated); Esc → exits vertex-edit (unchanged); Cmd-Z → restores via store `temporal()` middleware. `draw_polygon` mode for new polygons unaffected. **Verification.** `pnpm --filter @ogden/web typecheck` shows only 3 pre-existing unrelated errors (`StepBoundary.tsx:365`, two `HostUnion…` test files) — none in touched files. ADR: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete]]. - [2026-05-30 — B4 tooltip multi-pin (Slice L)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-multi-pin.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice L of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap. Retires the 2026-05-26 single-pin invariant: `pinnedUnion` (single `{ point, entries, hostIds }` object) replaced with `pinnedHosts: Map<string, HostBlock>` keyed by hostId; per-host click toggle, ESC + tap-outside clear ALL pins, single cursor-anchored stack merging pinned (insertion order, `pinned: true`) with hover (filtered by `!pinnedHosts.has`, `pinned: false`). `lastCursorPointRef` freezes the anchor when the cursor leaves canvas with pins active. Gold accent moves from container-level `.tooltip[data-pinned='true']` (border-color) to per-block `.hostBlock[data-pinned='true']` (2px gold left-border + 6px padding-left) so mixed pinned + hover stacks distinguish sticky from hover-along blocks at a glance. `HostBlockEntry` gains `pinned: boolean` (kept off `HostBlockProps` so the raw-data interface stays narrow); scroll-cap derivation moves from `!!pinned` to `entries.some(e => e.pinned)`. `sameHostIdSet()` helper deleted. **Use-case justification.** Roadmap required "design conversation about whether the use case (steward wanting to compare 2+ hosts side-by-side) is real before committing." Consulted **Permaculture Scholar NotebookLM (`5aa3dcf3-…`)** — unequivocal yes, citing four canonical permaculture design flows requiring simultaneous comparison of overlapping host canopies: (1) **50-year mature-canopy simulation** (spacing for tree A depends on B/C/D's mature spreads in the same frame); (2) **Edge maximization** (Holmgren P11 "Use Edges and Value the Marginal" — biodiversity concentrates in spaces *between* canopies; productive edge can't be designed one tree at a time); (3) **Cross-guild ecological aggregation** (N-fixers + dynamic accumulators + insectaries aggregate into coverage or redundancy — multi-guild question by definition); (4) **Suntrap / microclimate engineering** (U-shape / horseshoe arrangements creating sheltered microclimates — aggregate footprint + continuous shadow evaluated as a unit). Holmgren P8 ("Integrate Rather Than Segregate") underwrites all four. Single-pin was a segregation affordance working against P8. Scholar citations degenerate (~290 references to same handful of snippets — known indexer artifact); substantive claims hold independently against any permaculture-design textbook. **Key architectural choices.** `Map<hostId, HostBlock>` for O(1) per-host toggle + insertion-order iteration (newly-pinned at top of pinned section, consistent with 2026-05-27 topmost-first convention). Per-block accent not container-level so mixed stacks communicate sticky vs hover-along visually. `pinned` on `HostBlockEntry` not `HostBlockProps` (display-state, not raw-data payload). Single cursor-anchored stack rather than separate portals per pin (matches "these are the hosts I'm comparing" mental model). ESC + tap-outside clear ALL pins per roadmap recommendation ("get this off my screen" rarely scoped to one host). In-tooltip dismiss button OUT OF SCOPE — below Slice K's threshold=4 the tooltip is `pointer-events: none`, can't receive clicks without retiring the 2026-05-25 invariant; Slice M's drill-down surface (interactive by design) can ship it. **Tests.** Migrated test #3 from container-level `pinned` prop to per-entry; scroll-cap tests migrated to entry-level `pinned: true`. New `describe('multi-pin (Slice L)', ...)` with four cases: mixed pinned + hover (only pinned blocks carry data-pinned; root never carries data-pinned), all-pinned stack (every block carries data-pinned; separators between), all-hover stack (no data-pinned anywhere), scrollable regression guard (1 pinned + 3 hover = 4 ≥ threshold ⇒ scrollable because `entries.some` predicate, guarding against future tightening to "all pinned"). **Verification.** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers` → 28/28 (24 prior + 4 new). `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 288/288 (36 files; +4 over Slice N's 284). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files; pre-existing unrelated errors elsewhere unchanged. Preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree (Vite resolves against worktree-root `node_modules` which doesn't exist) — stated explicitly per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success." **Invariants preserved.** Slice K scroll-cap carve-out + tooltip-testid tap-outside exemption; Slice J / I / H; 2026-05-25 `pointer-events: none` in hover mode + pinned-small-stack; 2026-05-27 multi-feature fan-out (each feature toggles independently); 2026-05-28 ESC + tap-outside dismiss (semantics flip from "clear one" to "clear all"); 2026-05-29 / 30 fade machinery (`pinned` rides alongside `phase`); 2026-05-30 Slice N i18n seam (no new strings). **Invariant retired.** 2026-05-26 single-pin explicitly rolled back; ADR remains in wiki as historical context (defensive reasoning correct at the time, design question now answered). **Out of scope.** In-tooltip dismiss button (Slice M's space); pinned-count badge ("📌 N" header indicator — additive, defer); per-guild breakdown line inside a block (Slice O rejection deferred this to Slice M); persistence across page reloads (transient UI); keyboard navigation between pinned blocks (accessibility pass); integration tests for `PlanDataLayers` click-toggle Map logic (defer until a regression points at it). Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N + O + L shipped. **Remaining: Slice M** (hover-card drill-down — per-block click opens a richer surface listing per-guild breakdowns; depends on L's per-block addressability, which now exists).
- [2026-05-30 — B4 per-layer tinted stripe rejection (Slice O — second pass)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-per-layer-stripe-rejection.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice O of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap as a **documentation-only rejection** — no code change. The roadmap was explicit that this slice "must start with a research/decision step … decide whether the stripe is genuinely distinguishable (different surface) or re-introduces the same problem (same concept, different shape). Only then design the implementation, or document the second rejection with fresh reasoning." This slice ships the second-rejection path. **Prior rejections recap.** 2026-05-24 halo viz ADR colored the union halo neutral grey, explicitly rejecting `LAYER_TINT`: *"Neutral grey (not LAYER_TINT) because the union is a per-host aggregate, not a per-layer geometry; layer-tinting would mislead the eye into reading the halo as canopy-layer-specific."* 2026-05-25 hover tooltip ADR carried the reasoning forward to the tooltip stripe: *"the union is a per-host aggregate; layer-tinting would reintroduce the misleading-hue concern 2026-05-24 called out for the halo itself."* Both deferred as "revisit if needed." **Fresh counter-argument considered.** The natural revisit: the halo is on the map (color = layer-data), but the tooltip is a *separate UI surface* with its own visual conventions (already carries a gold "saved overlap" accent — a non-data color), so a stripe there would read as "category metadata," not as "this geometry = green-layer." **Why the counter-argument fails on two grounds.** (1) **Visual contiguity.** The tooltip is cursor-anchored adjacent to the halo it describes — stewards see them simultaneously. A green stripe next to a grey halo invites the eye to bind "this host = green," propagating the layer-tint association from the *label* onto the halo it labels. The surface boundary doesn't exist for the eye when the surfaces are positionally adjacent; the 2026-05-24 reasoning survives unchanged: the stripe tints the halo's label, which is the same problem one frame downstream. (2) **"Dominant" is the wrong reduction.** A host is in the silvopasture data because it carries *multiple* canopy layers (polyculture by construction). Every available definition of "dominant" elevates one layer above the others — biggest area biases toward fast-spreading shrubs, most members biases toward groundcovers, tallest requires schema work (data model doesn't track per-member heights), alphabetical is arbitrary and defensible only as a tie-breaker. Polyculture composition is the load-bearing feature of the model; hiding four-fifths of it behind one layer's color is a model violation, not a presentation choice. **What the steward actually needs (and where it goes).** The existing counts line — *"3 guilds · 7 canopy-bearing members"* — already surfaces polyculture composition. If at-a-glance per-layer breakdown matters, the right UI is a small list inside the tooltip (e.g. `overstory ×2 · midstory ×3 · understory ×2`), with each layer name in its own tint *as a label, not as a category color for the host as a whole*. **This breakdown is not in scope for Slice O** — it overlaps with **Slice M** (hover-card drill-down), where the natural design move is to expand a block into a richer surface that lists per-guild breakdowns. Whoever picks Slice M up next can lean on this ADR's reasoning to justify the breakdown approach. **Status flip.** 2026-05-24 / 25 ADRs left this as "deferred — revisit if needed." This slice flips it to **decided rejection**. Future roadmap sweeps should not re-list it as candidate work without the underlying constraint (silvopasture is polyculture-by-construction; "dominant layer" is information loss) materially changing. **Out of scope.** Code changes (none, by design); per-guild breakdown line in the tooltip text (Slice M's space); layer-aware *icons* on the tooltip (canopy/midstory/understory glyphs — distinct from color-tint, worth a separate design conversation); changes to the existing `LAYER_TINT` palette on the map's per-member geometries (those remain correct — per-member geometries genuinely belong to a single layer); light/dark theming (separate deferral). **Verification.** No code change → no tests to run, no tsc to check, no preview-server to verify. The slice's deliverable is this log entry + the ADR; both are reviewable in `git log`. **Invariants preserved.** Every B4 invariant from earlier ADRs holds verbatim — no surface has been touched. Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N shipped as code; **O shipped as a documented rejection**. Remaining: **Slice L** (multi-pin — substantial slice; needs design conversation about whether the "steward wants to compare 2+ hosts side-by-side" use case is real before committing) and **Slice M** (hover-card drill-down — depends on L's per-block addressability).
- [2026-05-30 — B4 tooltip i18n seam (Slice N)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-i18n-seam.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice N of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap by shipping the small-path option (path 2): extracts every English string the tooltip surfaces into a new colocated `tooltipStrings.ts` module with a clean seam for future i18next adoption, **without** bootstrapping i18next project-wide. **What changed.** New `apps/web/src/v3/plan/layers/tooltipStrings.ts`: `tooltipStrings` const object holds 3 row labels (`unionFootprint` = "Union footprint", `rawDiskSum` = "Raw π·r² sum", `savedOverlap` = "Saved overlap"); two formatter functions encapsulate the unit-suffix + pluralization logic — `formatAreaM2(n)` rounds + appends " m²", `formatHostCounts(guildCount, memberCount)` renders the counts line with English n===1 binary pluralization ("guild"/"guilds", "member"/"members"), the " · " separator, and the "canopy-bearing" qualifier all baked in. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` removes its inline `formatM2` helper, imports the three exports, swaps inline ternaries for the formatter call, and replaces bare string literals with `{tooltipStrings.unionFootprint}` etc. 6 formatter unit tests pin area rounding (incl. 0.49 → "0 m²" toward-zero edge) + plural/singular/zero-as-plural combinations. **Why path 2 not path 1.** `react-i18next` + `i18next` are deps but **zero** `useTranslation` / `i18n.init` call sites exist anywhere in `apps/web/src` — the tooltip would be the first consumer. Path 1 would force five ADR-worthy decisions in this slice's scope: bootstrap location, `<I18nextProvider>` wrapper near the app root (startup-time + pending Atlas-portal SSR consideration), resource-file layout (namespace boundaries), bundle-size assessment (~30kB gzipped naively bundled), and a project-wide copy-migration policy. The constants module gets the strings *organised* without forcing any of those bets; path 1 stays available as a follow-up when a second locale is confirmed. **Why a TS module, not a JSON resource file.** JSON is standard i18next layout but can't hold the formatter functions — splitting them now would leave a half-organised seam. When i18next lands, formatters become a thin shim around `t()` and the string-constant object migrates to JSON; the file shrinks or disappears. **Why keep English n===1 in-module.** A real i18n library will replace it with CLDR plural rules per locale (Arabic: six forms; Russian: three). Current formatter signature `(count, count) => string` is narrow on purpose — future swap to `t('tooltip.hostCounts', { guildCount, memberCount })` requires no call-site changes. **Migration recipe documented** in the module header docstring: (1) add `apps/web/src/i18n/index.ts` i18next bootstrap, (2) wrap `<App />` in `<I18nextProvider>`, (3) swap `tooltipStrings.foo` for `t('tooltip.foo')`, (4) move values into `locales/en/tooltip.json`, (5) delete the module. **Strings preserved byte-identically.** Row labels, " m²" suffix, " · " separator, "canopy-bearing" qualifier, n===1 binary pluralization — all unchanged. The existing tooltip rendering tests pass without modification, strong evidence the refactor changed nothing observable. **Verification.** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers` → 24/24 (12 tooltip + 6 memberDragMath + 6 new tooltipStrings); `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 284/284 (36 files; +6 over Slice K); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files; preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success" — refactor is a pure extraction whose visible output is byte-identical per the unchanged rendering tests. **Invariants preserved.** All Slice K (scroll-cap carve-out, data-scrollable threshold=4), J / I / H, and earlier B4 invariants (mouseleave-driven dismiss in hover mode + small-pinned, single-pin, multi-feature fan-out, touch tap-outside dismiss, enter + exit + per-block + reverse-in-flight fade, `prefers-reduced-motion`). **Out of scope.** Bootstrapping i18next (path 1, deferred); extracting strings from any other surface (tooltip-only by scope); number formatting beyond m² (decimal separators, grouping — available once i18next lands); RTL layout (separate infrastructure decision — CSS logical properties + `[dir]` attribute on `<html>`). Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N shipped; next is **Slice O** (per-layer tinted accent stripe — research/decision step first, may ship as a "still rejected" ADR rather than code) per the approved execution order.
- [2026-05-30 — B4 tooltip max-height scroll cap (Slice K)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-scroll-cap.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice K of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap — the highest-risk wave-C entry because **any** scroll affordance on the host-canopy-union tooltip requires `pointer-events: auto`, which collides with the 2026-05-25 invariant that the tooltip must NEVER steal the underlying union layer's mouseleave. **The carve-out.** `.tooltip[data-scrollable='true']` activates only when `pinned=true AND entries.length >= 4`. The CSS rule adds `max-height: calc(100vh - 80px)`, `overflow-y: auto`, and `pointer-events: auto`. Below either condition the invariant survives verbatim: hover mode + any host count = `pointer-events: none` and mouseleave-driven dismiss; pinned + 1–3 hosts = same. Above both conditions, mouseleave is moot — when pinned, dismissal is via ESC, click-again-on-host, or tap-outside-canvas-and-outside-tooltip, none of which depend on the tooltip's pointer-events. **Tap-outside handler carve-out (PlanDataLayers).** `onDocPointerDown` would have dismissed pointerdowns on the tooltip's scrollbar/content (target not in canvas → fall through). New early-return: `if (target instanceof Element && target.closest('[data-testid="host-canopy-union-tooltip"]')) return;`. The tooltip is portalled to the document body so PlanDataLayers can't hold a ref to it — the data-testid already used by tests becomes the production query selector, no portal-aware ref forwarding needed. **Edge-clamp adjustment.** Raw `entries.length * PER_BLOCK_H` would over-reserve vertical space when the surface is scroll-capped (e.g. 20-host pinned stack) and push the anchor unnecessarily high; new `scrollCapMaxH = Math.max(PER_BLOCK_H, viewportH - 80)` bounds the estimatedH when `scrollable`. `Math.max(PER_BLOCK_H, ...)` guards against pathologically short viewports. **Threshold = 4.** Three hosts (~340px) fits 768px viewport comfortably; four (~448px) tight; five+ clips. Single `SCROLL_CAP_THRESHOLD = 4` module constant so a future tuning round can move it without touching consumers. **Reserve = 80px.** `calc(100vh - 80px)` matches the existing edge-clamp's intuitive budget (12px cursor gap + 8px padding at top/bottom + DesignToolRail headroom); on a 720px viewport ~640px usable ≈ 5.9 blocks, "scroll if you must" not "scroll constantly." **Why not WAAPI / wheel-capture.** The roadmap's alternative — capture `wheel` events on the document, translate to a CSS-variable offset on a virtual scrollable container — would preserve the 2026-05-25 invariant verbatim but re-implement overscroll, inertia, scrollbar-drag, keyboard scroll, and require a separate `touchmove` path for tablets. The dual carve-out (CSS + tap-outside) ships in ~10 lines and inherits every native scroll affordance for free; the narrow carve-out window keeps the invariant holding in every state the steward meets during normal hover flow. **Why threshold-by-entry-count not viewport-bound.** The cleaner predicate would be `scrollable = pinned && rawEstimatedH > scrollCapMaxH`, but (a) entries.length is stable across viewport changes (resize doesn't toggle the carve-out under a pinned steward) and (b) the test surface stays simpler. If the fixed threshold proves wrong for small viewports, swap the predicate without changing the data-attribute contract. **Reused, not built:** existing portal mount; existing data-testid; existing tap-outside listener; existing edge-clamp logic; existing fade machinery (data-visible / data-exiting / transition tokens). **Tests added:** 4 under `scroll-cap carve-out (Slice K)` describe — below-threshold pinned = no data-scrollable; above-threshold unpinned = no data-scrollable (hover invariant survives); at-threshold pinned = data-scrollable='true'; very-tall (20-host) pinned at viewport-top = data-scrollable='true' + edge-clamp produces non-negative top (regression guard). **Verification:** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers/__tests__/HostCanopyUnionTooltip.test.tsx` → 12/12 (8 prior + 4 new); `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 278/278 (35 files; +4 over Slice J); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on the three touched files (pre-existing unrelated errors elsewhere unchanged); preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success" — data-attribute contract fully unit-test-covered, visible scroll relies on browser-native `overflow-y: auto`. **Invariants preserved:** 2026-05-25 (mouseleave-driven dismiss in hover mode + pinned-small-stack), 2026-05-26 (single-pin), 2026-05-27 (multi-feature fan-out), 2026-05-28 (touch tap-outside dismiss), 2026-05-29 + 30 (enter + exit + per-block + reverse-in-flight fade), `prefers-reduced-motion`. **Out of scope:** Slice L multi-pin (separate slice; depends on this one), Slice M hover-card drill-down (depends on L), viewport-aware predicate, sticky block headers when scrolling, keyboard arrow-key navigation between blocks. Roadmap status: H + I + J + K shipped; next is **Slice N** (tooltip i18n small path) per the approved execution order.
- [2026-05-30 — B4 InlineFeaturePopover exit fade (Slice J)](log/2026-05-30-b4-inline-popover-exit-fade.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice J of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap, consuming the `--motion-overlay-*` tokens added in Slice I. Click-driven inline mini-form `InlineFeaturePopover` adopts the same deferred-unmount machinery the 2026-05-30 host-canopy-union tooltip ship landed: a `displayed: InlineFormPayload | null` mirror state lives one exit-transition longer than `useInlineFormStore.active`, `exiting: boolean` flips at the same time `active` goes null, `visible: boolean` flips via `useLayoutEffect` after mount so the enter transition fires from `opacity: 0`/`translateY(2px)` → `opacity: 1`/`translateY(0)`. CSS-Module `.popover` rule gains the from-state + `transition: opacity var(--motion-overlay-duration) var(--motion-overlay-ease-out), transform var(--motion-overlay-duration) var(--motion-overlay-ease-out)`. New `.popover[data-visible='true']` selector targets the visible state; new `.popover[data-exiting='true']` mirrors the from-state, switches the easing token to `--motion-overlay-ease-in`, and adds **`pointer-events: none`** so a mid-fade click on a fading Save/Cancel button is physically impossible. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` block nulls both transitions so reduced-motion users see instant dismissal. **The interactivity invariant difference from the tooltip.** Tooltip is `pointer-events: none` — invariant: "must never steal events from the underlying layer." Popover is `pointer-events: auto` — owns inputs, Save, Cancel, custom actions. So the tooltip's invariant doesn't transfer. New invariant: **a mid-fade click on a fading button must not race the displayed-mirror cleanup.** Defense-in-depth: exit-state CSS drops `pointer-events: none` (primary defence), Save/Cancel handlers also guard on `if (!active)` (free insurance — store entry has cleared by the time exit starts). **Value-reset block now skips active=null.** Pre-fade logic unconditionally cleared `values` when `active` went null; with deferred unmount the form renders through the fade and clearing values mid-fade would visually empty every input. New logic only resets when active becomes a **new non-null payload**; active going null is the exit signal and values stay frozen until `displayed` clears. **`onPopoverTransitionEnd` filters on three conditions.** `propertyName === 'opacity'` (rejects the transform-property transitionend so the unmount is deterministic and tied to the visually-disappearing property), `target === currentTarget` (rejects bubbled child transitionends from nested `<input>`, `<select>`, `<button>` focus-ring + hover-state transitions), `exiting === true` (rejects post-reverse-in-flight transitionends that would spuriously unmount a restored form). 200ms safety `setTimeout` covers `prefers-reduced-motion` where transitionend never fires. **Render guard switched from `if (!active) return null` → `if (!displayed) return null`** so the form stays mounted through the fade; title, fields, customActions iteration all read from `displayed`. New 4-test suite `InlineFeaturePopover.test.tsx` pins: cold-start renders nothing; `open()` mounts with `data-visible='true'`; `close()` flips `data-exiting='true'`, transform-property transitionend does NOT unmount but opacity-property transitionend does; reverse-in-flight `open()` during exit restores form and subsequent opacity transitionend does not spuriously unmount. Uses the same `fireTransitionEnd(el, propertyName)` `Object.defineProperty` happy-dom helper as the 2026-05-30 tooltip tests. **Reused, not built:** Slice I `--motion-overlay-*` tokens; deferred-unmount pattern from the 2026-05-30 tooltip ship; existing ESC + click-outside listeners (still gated on `active` so they auto-detach at exit start — correct, because the form is no longer interactive). **Invariants preserved:** schema-driven render (title, fields, customActions, required-field gate, disclosure expansion) unchanged; ESC + click-outside dismiss; reduced-motion behaviour. **Out of scope:** the slide-up dialog used for written reports (different surface class — slide-up animation, not fade); cubic-bezier alignment of overlay surfaces with the project's `--ease-out`/`--ease-in` family (deferred per the Slice I ADR; revisit when a third consumer arrives); per-field exit animations within the popover. **Verification:** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 274/274 green (35 files; +4 new InlineFeaturePopover tests; 8/8 tooltip tests untouched); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files (pre-existing unrelated errors in `LandAssessmentSlideUp.tsx`, `AtlasAIPanel.tsx`, `HydrologyRightPanel.tsx` confirmed unchanged via baseline grep); preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree (Vite resolves against worktree-root `node_modules` which doesn't exist) — stated explicitly per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success," structurally identical to the 2026-05-30 tooltip ship whose contract is fully unit-test-covered. Roadmap status: H + I + J shipped; next is **Slice K** (max-height scroll cap when N hosts is large) which carries the `pointer-events` carve-out risk.
- [2026-05-30 — B4 motion-token harmonisation (Slice I)](log/2026-05-30-b4-motion-token-harmonisation.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice I of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap. Extracts the four hard-coded overlay-fade literals from `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.module.css` (duration `120ms`, translate `2px`, easing `ease-out`/`ease-in`) into a new `--motion-overlay-*` token family declared on `:root` in [apps/web/src/styles/tokens.css](../apps/web/src/styles/tokens.css) alongside the existing `--duration-*` / `--ease-*` families. Four sites of `transition: opacity 120ms ease-... , transform 120ms ease-...` rewritten as `var(...)` calls; three `translateY(2px)` sites likewise. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` block unchanged (nulls `transition` entirely, no per-token override needed). **Why a new family, not reuse `--duration-*` / `--ease-*`.** Existing duration ladder is 100/200/400/600ms; tooltip's 120ms was tuned because 100ms felt snappy and 200ms felt draggy under cursor motion. Existing `--ease-out`/`--ease-in` are cubic-beziers (`cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)` / `cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)`); tooltip ships with bare CSS keywords (`cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.58, 1)` / `cubic-bezier(0.42, 0, 1, 1)`). Coercing to either would ship a visual change as part of a "token extraction" slice. New family preserves literals verbatim; cubic-bezier alignment deferred to a follow-up ADR after Slice J's adoption verifies the current curves feel right with two consumers. **Why CSS custom properties, not TS constants.** CSS Modules can't reference TS without inline `style={{}}` (loses scoping) or a CSS-in-JS pipeline (overkill for four literals). The 200ms safety timeout in `PlanDataLayers.tsx` does duplicate `--motion-overlay-duration + slack`, but the slack is the load-bearing part — if a second JS consumer materialises we'll revisit. **Why these four tokens specifically.** Two easings (not one) because enter accelerates toward the visible state and exit decelerates away from it; CSS variables can't carry direction. One duration (not three) because the 2026-05-30 ship uses 120ms across enter / exit / reverse-in-flight — different durations per intent would be a design change, not extraction. **Tokens.css is already imported once at the app root via [app/index.css:6](../apps/web/src/app/index.css), so no additional wiring needed and CSS custom properties propagate through the cascade into CSS-Modules-scoped class names.** Tests untouched — contract tests only assert data-attrs + event handling, neither affected by value extraction. 8/8 tooltip + 63/63 agroforestry green. Touched files TS-clean. **Unlocks Slice J** (InlineFeaturePopover exit fade) which can adopt the same tokens at birth so the two map-overlay surfaces fade in sync. Roadmap deferrals: cubic-bezier alignment, dark-mode-only overrides, additional surface-class families (`--motion-modal-*` etc) all kept deferred.

- [2026-05-30 — B4 follow-up: per-block tooltip fade + reverse-in-flight](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-perblock-fade-and-reverse.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the last two still-deferred bullets from the 2026-05-29 exit-fade ADR: per-block exit fade in multi-host stacks, and reverse-in-flight animation when `activeUnion` returns non-null mid-exit. Fade machinery refactored from CSS keyframes (`@keyframes tooltipFadeIn` / `tooltipFadeOut`) to **CSS transitions** on opacity + transform; `.tooltip` mounts at `opacity: 0` and `.tooltip[data-visible='true']` flips to `opacity: 1` (the enter transition fires from a `useLayoutEffect` that sets `visible=true` on mount); `.tooltip[data-exiting='true']` takes opacity back to 0 with `ease-in` timing. New `.hostBlock` rule mirrors the same shape for per-block fades. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` override nulls all four selectors' `transition`. **Reverse-in-flight is free** with transitions: removing `data-exiting` mid-fade lets the transition interpolate from the current visible value back to 1, with no snap and no JS — making the 2026-05-29 monotonic-key remount pattern unnecessary. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` exports a new `HostBlockEntry` interface (hostId + per-entry `phase: 'entering' | 'exiting'`); `HostBlock` renders `data-testid='host-block-${hostId}'`, `data-exiting='true'` when phase==='exiting', and an `onTransitionEnd` filtered by `propertyName==='opacity'` + `target===currentTarget` that fires a new `onEntryExited?: (hostId: string) => void` prop. Container's own `onTransitionEnd` filters by both `propertyName==='opacity'` and `target===currentTarget` so bubbled per-block transitionends don't fire `onExited`. **Merge-by-hostId.** `PlanDataLayers.displayedUnion` state shape replaces 2026-05-29's `key + entries: HostBlock[]` with per-entry phase tracking (`entries: HostBlockEntry[]`); the monotonic key is gone. The mirror `useEffect` rewrites the merge: kept hosts (in both old and new sets) carry forward with phase `entering` and refreshed data; dropped hosts (in old but not new) flip to phase `exiting` and stay in the array; new hosts are appended in MapLibre topmost-first order. The React `key` on the rendered map iterator is now `entry.hostId` (stable per host) so a block's in-flight transition isn't cancelled when siblings drop out and the array re-indexes. `onEntryExited` callback drops the hostId from the entries array — or clears the mirror entirely if the last block just finished fading. Safety timeout bumped 180 → 200 ms (120 ms transition + 80 ms slack to absorb event-loop jitter and the `prefers-reduced-motion` instant-change case where transitionend doesn't fire). **Test scaffolding.** New `fireTransitionEnd(el, propertyName)` helper — `@testing-library/dom`'s `createEvent.transitionEnd` passes init to the constructor without a fallback, and happy-dom's `TransitionEvent` constructor silently drops the `propertyName` init key, so the helper `Object.defineProperty`'s the value onto the event post-construction. Existing tests migrated from `fireEvent.animationEnd({ animationName: 'tooltipFadeOut' })` to the new helper. Two new tests: reverse-in-flight asserts that flipping `exiting` from true → false during re-render clears `data-exiting` and a subsequent opacity transitionend does NOT fire `onExited`; per-block exit asserts that an entry with `phase='exiting'` carries `data-exiting='true'`, that opacity transitionend fires `onEntryExited(hostId)`, and that sibling `entering` blocks + transform-property transitionends do not. **Why transitions, not WAAPI.** The 2026-05-29 ADR speculated about `element.animate()` + `animation.reverse()`. Transitions get the same behaviour with zero JS: they always interpolate from the current computed value, which is exactly what "reverse" means for a single-property fade. **Why merge by hostId.** When the active set shrinks, the dropped host has to stay in the displayed array long enough to fade; indices shift under set changes, so a key-by-index would cancel its transition when the array re-reconciled. Invariants preserved: `pointer-events: none`, single-pin model, ESC + tap-outside-to-dismiss, multi-feature fan-out (2026-05-27), edge-clamp + entries-aware `ESTIMATED_H` (counts every block including phase-`exiting` ones so a tooltip about to lose a block stays clamped conservatively — no flicker-reposition mid-fade), reduced-motion behaviour (was: no keyframe animation; now: no transition). 71/71 vitest green (8 tooltip + 63 agroforestry; +2 tooltip tests over the 2026-05-29 ship). Touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-29 ADR reverse-in-flight + per-block bullets flipped open → closed.

- [2026-05-21 — fix(web): Vite dev proxy translates ECONNREFUSED into API_OFFLINE envelope](log/2026-05-21-vite-proxy-api-offline-envelope.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the "Response not JSON (500)" papercut on `POST /api/v1/auth/register` from `http://localhost:5200/login`. Confirmed via `Test-NetConnection` + direct `/health` probe that nothing was listening on port 3001; the 500 was Vite's dev proxy returning plain-text HTML for `ECONNREFUSED`, not the API (whose global `setErrorHandler` in `apps/api/src/app.ts` *always* sends a JSON envelope, so a non-JSON 500 cannot originate there). Added `configure` + `proxy.on('error', …)` to the `/api` entry in `apps/web/vite.config.ts` that emits a `503` carrying the API's own envelope shape `{ data: null, error: { code: 'API_OFFLINE', message: "API server unreachable at http://localhost:3001 (<errno>). Start it with:  pnpm --filter @ogden/api dev" } }`. `apiClient.ts` flows the envelope through unchanged → LoginPage `role="alert"` banner renders the actionable instruction verbatim. Iterated once on the message format — first draft wrapped the command in backticks; when an operator pasted the banner verbatim into PowerShell, the backticks parsed as line-continuation and `(ECONNREFUSED)` as a sub-expression call. Plain-text form is copy-paste safe. Verified in live preview: API stopped → in-page `fetch('/api/v1/auth/register')` returned `503` + envelope, LoginPage banner DOM matched verbatim, console error stream flipped from `ApiError: Response not JSON (500)` to `ApiError: API server unreachable …` at the moment Vite picked up the config change; API restarted → same call returned `201` + `{ token, user }`. No edits to auth routes (`apps/api/src/routes/auth/index.ts` was sound), no new migrations, no dev seed-user script (explicitly declined — permanent fix only). ADR: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-vite-proxy-api-offline-envelope]].

- [2026-05-29 — B4 follow-up: tooltip exit fade](log/2026-05-29-b4-tooltip-exit-fade.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the last fade-related still-deferred bullet from the 2026-05-25 host-union-hover-tooltip ADR (deferred again on 2026-05-28): animated fade **out**. `PlanDataLayers.tsx` gets a third `useState` (`displayedUnion`) that mirrors `activeUnion = pinnedUnion ?? hoveredUnion` but lives one exit-animation longer, with `phase: 'entering' | 'exiting'` and a monotonic `key`. A `useEffect([activeUnion])` writes the mirror synchronously on non-null `activeUnion` (fresh `key` remounts the tooltip so the enter keyframe replays — covers re-enter during in-flight exit) and flips the mirror's phase to `'exiting'` on null `activeUnion`. A 180 ms safety `setTimeout` (120 ms anim + 60 ms slack) covers the `prefers-reduced-motion` short-circuit case where `animationend` never fires. Portal-render now reads `displayedUnion`, forwards `key`, `exiting`, and `onExited`, and forces `pinned={false}` during exit so the gold accent doesn't linger. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` props extended with optional `exiting?` + `onExited?`; root `<div>` gets conditional `data-exiting='true'` and an `onAnimationEnd` handler that fires `onExited()` when `exiting === true` and `animationName.includes('tooltipFadeOut')` (CSS Modules scopes the keyframe name; `.includes` matches the scoped form). `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.module.css` adds `@keyframes tooltipFadeOut` (opacity 1→0, translateY 0→2px — the reverse of the enter keyframe); `.tooltip[data-exiting='true'] { animation: tooltipFadeOut 120ms ease-in forwards; }` — `forwards` holds the final state until React unmount. The `prefers-reduced-motion` media block extended to null both keyframes. New test asserts `data-exiting` forwarding + `onExited` fires on `tooltipFadeOut` animationend and NOT on unrelated keyframe names. Why not `useRef` or `useReducer`: refs don't trigger re-render (the portal-branch needs to subscribe); two-shape state machine doesn't justify reducer boilerplate. Why force `pinned=false` during exit: gold accent reads "sticky," fade reads "going away" — stacking confuses the surface. Invariants preserved: `pointer-events: none`, single-pin, single-tooltip, multi-feature fan-out, edge-clamp, enter fade, tap-outside dismiss. 69/69 vitest green (6 tooltip + 63 agroforestry). Touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-25 + 2026-05-28 ADR exit-fade bullets flipped to closed.

- [2026-05-20 — Phase C: Agent workforce + rotation→revenue bridge](log/2026-05-20-phase-c-agent-workforce-rotation-engine.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Two commits closing the Apricot-Lane Phase C boundary. **C.6 (`8418062a`)** widens `ClaudeClient.callAnthropic` to accept a `string | SystemBlock[]` and widens the return shape to `{ text, model, inputTokens, outputTokens }` (zero impact on the three existing public callers — string is wrapped in a single ephemeral-cached block as today). `SYSTEM_PROMPT` exported. New public `ClaudeClient.chatWithRole({ roleSystemAddendum, userMessage })` builds the canonical 2-block array — `[0]` cached Atlas base prompt with `cache_control: { type: 'ephemeral' }`, `[1]` the role addendum — and delegates to `callAnthropic`. New `apps/api/src/services/ai/agentRegistry.ts` exports `AgentRole` (`'agro-designer' | 'hydro-engineer' | 'general'`), a static role-prompt table, pure `routeIntent(text): AgentRole` (case-insensitive word-boundary keyword tally — hydro: `swale`, `keyline`, `pond`, `water`, `hydro`, `runoff`, `infiltration`, `drainage`, `riparian`, `aquifer`, `cistern`, `dam`, `creek`, `flood`; agro: `orchard`, `paddock`, `tree`, `plant`, `species`, `crop`, `pasture`, `grazing`, `livestock`, `rotation`, `cover crop`, `compost`, `silvopasture`; ties or zero → `'general'`), `resolveRole`, and `runAgent(input)` which composes the role addendum, calls `chatWithRole`, and parses any trailing `HANDOFF: <role> — <reason>` line (en-dash `—` or ASCII `--` separator) into `handoff: { to, reason } | null` (server does not auto-chain — caller decides). New route `POST /api/v1/ai/agent-chat` appended to `apps/api/src/routes/ai/index.ts` with `authenticate + resolveProjectRole` preHandlers (project-membership gate). 24-case test suite `apps/api/src/tests/aiAgents.test.ts` mirrors the `ClaudeClient.test.ts` global-`fetch`-stub pattern: `routeIntent` purity, `parseHandoff` positives + negatives + ASCII separator + malformed role, `resolveRole` precedence, `runAgent` end-to-end (composes the 2-block system array with the cached base prompt verbatim, autoRoutes, defaults to general, parses handoff, forwards usage tokens) and a direct `chatWithRole` unit test. **C.7 (`6a61d6cf`)** lands `apps/web/src/features/livestock/engine/rotationEngine.ts` (`computeRotationCalendar({ paddocks, herdSize, animalUnitMonths?, parasiteBreakDays = 60, grazeDaysPerPaddock = 3 }): RotationCalendar`) — wraps canonical `computeRotationCarryingCapacity` via a synthetic single-mob `RotationPlan` (every paddock in one cell group, `targetGrazeDays = grazeDaysPerPaddock`, `targetRestDays = parasiteBreakDays`) plus mob-grazed paddock list with per-paddock `stockingDensity = herdSize / areaHa` so the AU math is never forked; `cycleDays = grazeDaysPerPaddock × paddocks.length`; `recoveryDays = cycleDays − grazeDaysPerPaddock`; `annualAuDays = herdSize × 365`; `cyclesPerYear = floor(365 / cycleDays)`; `parasiteBreakCompliant = every entry's recoveryDays ≥ parasiteBreakDays`; degenerate input (no paddocks or `grazeDaysPerPaddock ≤ 0`) returns a well-formed zero calendar (`entries: []`, `cycleDays: 0`, `cyclesPerYear: 0`, vacuously compliant, `status: 'ok'`). New `apps/web/src/features/financial/engine/livestockRevenue.ts` (`buildLivestockRevenueStream(calendar, { pricePerAuDay, startYear = 1, maturityYear?, confidence = 'medium', assumptions?, id?, name? })`) — `annualRevenue.{low,mid,high} = pricePerAuDay.{...} × annualAuDays` (rounded); default 5-year build-up ramp `[0.2, 0.4, 0.65, 0.85, 1.0]` plateauing at 1.0 through year 10; `startYear` shifts the ramp; `assumptions[]` surfaces herd × 365 AU-days, rotation cycle + paddock count, parasite-break compliance line (✓ "Parasite-break floor met (Xd minimum rest)" vs ✗ "WARNING: parasite-break floor NOT met — recovery Yd < Xd"), utilization + status, plus caller-supplied lines; default `enterprise: 'livestock'`. The stream slots into `computeCashflow([], [stream], phases, horizon)` with **zero engine change**. `RotationScheduleCard.tsx` gains an additive "Cycle engine" summary block between the status pills row and the per-group timelines: `cyclesPerYear`, `annualAuDays` (locale-formatted), parasite-break compliance badge (green ≥ 60d / amber < 60d), and utilization % with status pill (`ok` / `tight` / `over`). Card doesn't track herd size today, so the block uses an implied-mob heuristic of ~1 AU/ha (`Math.max(1, round(totalHa))`) — clearly labelled in the header hint so stewards know it's a placeholder until herd-size capture lands. Existing ad-hoc moves table below is untouched per [[feedback_no_deletion]]; plan-driven `RotationSequenceCard.tsx` is left alone. 16 new tests (8 rotation-engine + 8 livestock-revenue) cover: 11 × 3-day graze → `cycleDays 33`, `recoveryDays 30`, parasite-break NOT met; 11 × 6-day graze → `cycleDays 66`, `recoveryDays 60`, compliant; 50 AU × 365 = 18,250 AU-days; 200-acre fixture at 1 AU / 2 acres → 36,500 AU-days; contiguous startDay sequence; degenerate empty + zero-herd paths; utilization roll-up; `annualRevenue.mid = pricePerAuDay.mid × annualAuDays`; enterprise tag; ramp 0 before startYear + monotone non-decreasing through plateau; startYear shift; WARNING / Parasite-break-floor-met assumptions; end-to-end `computeCashflow` integration (year-0 = 0, year-1 > 0, year-10 ≥ year-1). Gate: API tsc clean; `pnpm --filter @ogden/api run test` **653 passed / 3 skipped (656)** across 60 files; web tsc shows only pre-existing `StepBoundary.tsx(365,7)` `unknown→ReactNode` foreign-WIP error (verified via stash-baseline comparison); `pnpm --filter @ogden/web run test` **1620 passed (1620)** across 157 files (incl. 24 C.6 + 16 C.7 new cases). Manual 200-acre fixture smoke deferred per Assumption A2. Covenant + IA preserved: no CSRA / *bayʿ mā laysa ʿindak* / salam framing reintroduced; "capital partners & allies" language preserved (livestock revenue is steward-facing operating estimate, not investor yield); 3-item Observe/Plan/Act IA unchanged; mobile Overview stack stays flat (engine block lands on the card, not the mobile shell). ADR: [[decisions/2026-05-20-atlas-phase-c-agent-workforce-rotation-engine]]. - [2026-05-27 — B4 follow-up: multi-feature fan-out on host-union tooltip](log/2026-05-27-b4-union-tooltip-multi-feature-fanout.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the "Multi-feature fan-out when `resolveSilvopastureHosts` ever produces overlapping hosts" still-deferred bullet on the 2026-05-25 host-union-hover-tooltip ADR. The 2026-05-25 + 2026-05-26 ships both read only `e.features?.[0]` — when two silvopasture polygons spatially overlap (silvopastureHosts enumerator unions cropAreas + designElements with no dedup), the steward sees only one host's three m² values. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip` props refactored: new exported `HostBlockProps` interface; top-level shape becomes `{ point, entries: HostBlockProps[], pinned? }` (flat single-host fields removed, no backward-compat shim). Render loops `entries.map((e, i) => ...)` with `<hr className={styles.separator} role="separator" />` between consecutive blocks (single-host stacks omit the separator entirely — visually identical to the 2026-05-26 ship). `HostBlock` sub-component lifted local to the file. Edge-clamp `ESTIMATED_H` now `entries.length`-aware (`BASE_H + entries.length * PER_BLOCK_H` ~ 16 + 108·n) so the bottom-edge anchor flip keeps a 3-block tooltip on-screen at the gutter. CSS adds `.separator` hairline rule (`#f2ede3` family at 0.12 opacity against the dark glass). `PlanDataLayers` state widened: `hoveredUnion` / `pinnedUnion` carry `entries: HostBlock[]` (`HostBlock = HostBlockProps & { hostId: string }`); pinned additionally keeps a sorted `hostIds: string[]` for set-equality unpin. `unpackProps` → `unpackEntries` walks every entry in `e.features` (not `[0]`), filters by `properties.kind === 'host-canopy-union'`, dedups by `hostId` via `Set` (MapLibre can emit the same Feature twice when its source has multiple visible tiles intersecting the cursor). Click toggle now uses `sameHostIdSet` sorted-array equality: clicking a stack whose `hostIds` set matches the pinned stack's unpins; any other click replaces. Hover-suppression-while-pinned and ESC unpin unchanged. Portal render forwards `entries` instead of spread props. Why vertical stack, not tabs / chooser: any in-tooltip interactivity (tabs, hover-card-to-expand, chooser) would force `pointer-events: auto` and break the 2026-05-25 non-negotiable that the tooltip never steals `mouseleave` from the underlying union-fill. Stacking is the only design that holds the invariant. 1 new render test (two-host stack: both names visible, both sets of m² values rendered, exactly one `role="separator"` between); 4 existing tests migrated to length-1 `entries`. 5/5 tooltip + 63/63 agroforestry green; touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-25 ADR's multi-feature-fan-out bullet flipped open → closed.

- [2026-05-21 — Habitat-feature unification into Plan design elements (Slices 1-3 landed then dropped by external rebase, Slice 4 partial)](log/2026-05-21-habitat-feature-unification-into-design-elements.md) — Steward-chosen direction for the A2 habitat commitments (owl/nest boxes, raptor perches, hedgerows, insectary strips, brush piles, snags, wildlife ponds): unify into Plan `DesignElement` subtypes under a new `habitat` category in `elementCatalog.ts`. Three slices landed and verified — **Slice 1** (`43dd56a9`) new category + 7 first-class kinds (`owl-box` / `raptor-perch` / `nest-box` / `brush-pile` / `snag` / `insectary-strip` / `wetland-edge`) + 6 colour tokens + Lucide icons + explicit tool-dispatch switch cases (discovered against plan assumption: dispatch is NOT fully catalog-driven), template-literal arm on `MapToolId`, `TOOL_GROUPS` `'habitat-allocation'` rail; **Slice 2** (`933c0709`) optional `habitatMetadata?` slot on `DesignElement` (scoped down from per-kind popover — schema-only suffices for all four downstream consumers); **Slice 3** (`ac11dfa6`) extends `BeneficialStructureKind` + `BENEFICIAL_STRUCTURE_FUNCTIONS` with cited categories for each new kind (Cornell NestWatch / Audubon Working Lands / USDA NRCS / USDA Forest Service PNW-GTR-181 / Xerces CSP 422 — preserves B5 cite-every-claim covenant) and adds 7 new aggregate fields + 7 new structural-loop arms to `beneficialHabitatMath`, updating `structuralPoints` to `hedgerowM/100 + pondM²/500 + shrubs + owlBoxes + raptorPerches + nestBoxes + brushPiles + snags + insectaryStripM/100 + wetlandEdgeM²/500`; envelope clamp unchanged so effect on existing projects is monotonic increase. 37 vitest specs added across catalog + math suites, all green at commit time. **Slice 4** (uncommitted) introduced pure-selector module `apps/web/src/features/biodiversity/habitatCommitments.ts` (10-kind `HabitatCommitmentTally` shape via turf line-length / polygon-area helpers) with 10-spec colocated test, an additive "Planned habitat commitments" sub-panel on `BiodiversityMonitorCard`, and a read-only "Placed on map" summary block at the top of `FeatureInventoryPanel` (legacy scalar add-form retained as soft-deprecated path; destructive v1→v2 bridge migration deliberately skipped to keep the slice rebase-safe). **Slice 5** (D0 spine seeder via `habitatFeatureSpineSync.ts`) not started. After commits landed, an external interactive rebase replayed `feat/atlas-permaculture` onto a new base and dropped all three slice commits from the resulting history (the exact failure mode [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]] warns about — committed work survives rebases unless a pick is explicitly dropped, which here it was); Slice 4 file edits + the two new untracked files were also wiped by the subsequent hard-reset. Local now matches `origin/feat/atlas-permaculture` exactly. Re-application path: plan checked into `~/.claude/plans/habitat-features-need-a-lively-oasis.md`, file inventory in the linked log entry, all per-file content documented.

- [2026-06-02 -- Observe lens: fix viewport fill + restructure chrome](log/2026-06-02-atlas-observe-lens-fill-restructure.md) -- Operator review of the promotion reported the lens confined to ~58% of the viewport (`C.bg` gutters right + bottom) and asked to rearrange the chrome. Fill: the zoom box used `width/height: calc(100%/Z)`, assuming the older Chromium semantics where `zoom` scales the box footprint; this engine fills the percentage box and zoom only magnifies internal lengths, so the calc double-shrank the UI -- fixed by `width/height: 100%` (min font still 12px). The `module-bar` branch also drops `StageShell` for a full-bleed `absolute; inset:0` mount (the grid/flex context was a second confinement source); `dashboard` branch byte-untouched. Chrome: `CycleTimelineBar` gains a `vertical` always-expanded left-sidebar mode (spiral + cycle header + Now/Observe callout + signals); `DomainsView` gains a `horizontal` scroll-x top-bar mode (rich lens cards, now the sole lens selector); `LensBar` removed from root JSX (`LensBar`/`DomainsRail` left defined-but-unused, no-deletion); `IntelligencePanel` unchanged right. Mock-backed; `tsc --noEmit` exit 0; verified live on a module-bar project (0 `C.bg` gutters across 75 edge samples, zoom box fills 1266x916, card-click drives `activeLens` via React fiber, screenshot captured, dashboard-shell diff empty). Explicit-path commit `bcb0ea2b` (3 files), not pushed. ADR [[decisions/2026-06-02-atlas-observe-lens-fill-restructure]].

- [2026-06-04 -- OLOS Act completion unification (Phase 1): formal panel into the tier-shell](log/2026-06-04-olos-act-completion-unification-phase1.md) -- First shippable step of the `ObserveDataPoint` replacement migration ([[decisions/2026-06-04-olos-proof-verification-fork]]). The kickoff slice mounted the formal proof/verification panel only in `ActFeedbackLoop` (OLOS workspace); this phase surfaces it inside the **tier-shell** completion surface (`ActTierExecutionPanel` right rail) behind the same default-off `isOlosFormalProofEnabled()` flag, unifying the two Act-completion surfaces. The crux: the two models use **different id spaces** -- lightweight keys `ObserveDataPoint.sourceObjectiveId` to per-project `PlanStratumObjective.id`; formal keys `ActTask.objectiveId` to the **universal** catalogue Act objective id (`${domain}--act`). Bridged by **domain only**, never id-equality: pure `resolveActObjectiveId(objective)` (`packages/shared/.../actObjectiveTaskBridge.ts`) + read-only store-aware `useActObjectiveTaskBridge` returning `{status:'offline'|'no-domain'|'no-task'|'ready', actObjectiveId, tasks}` (no writes, no auto-seed -- synced-but-no-task shows a "No formal task yet" hint since tier-shell objectives carry no `ActHandoffPackage` and `ActTaskSchema` requires `handoffPackageId` min 1). On a formal PASS the tier-shell adapter emits a `task_verification` `ObserveDataPoint` keyed to the objective's `domainId` + `sourceObjectiveId` (matching the lightweight path exactly so it slots into the existing Observe rollup) via a new optional `onVerifiedPass?(verification)` callback on `TaskProofPanel` (fired only on pass; OLOS-workspace mount leaves it unset). `TaskProofPanel` restyled to a dedicated theme-variable-driven `TaskProofPanel.module.css` (panel-scoped `--tpp-*` tokens resolved from a host-variable fallback chain so it inherits warm/gold tier-shell vs cool/blue OLOS). Invariants: flag-off byte-identical (all new JSX flag-gated, bridge pure-read), offline = lightweight, no schema/API/route change, lightweight "Record observation" kept as permanent offline fallback. Bounded vitest: shared bridge 4/4, hook 6/6, TaskProofPanel 6/6, `ActTierExecutionPanel.formal` 5/5; full tier-shell dir 78 pass (the 5 `ActTierExecutionPanel.protocols.test.tsx` failures are PRE-EXISTING, same count as baseline -- a trigger-recognition regression flagged for separate triage). Web `tsc` clean outside pre-existing `src/compost/`. **Live e2e smoke NOT YET RUN.** Explicit-path commits `b960f159` -> `339284a3` -> `18538b55` -> `ff6a3c16` -> `fb818a80` -> docs, not pushed ([[project-branch-rebase]]); HEAD moved externally mid-session so pathspec commits used throughout. Deferred: retire `recordDataPoint` for completion, flip flag default, per-type capture affordances, OLOS-workspace `task_verification` emission. ADR [[decisions/2026-06-04-olos-proof-verification-fork]] (Phase 1 section). Amanah: evidence capture only, no sales/finance instrument -- clean.

Auth code was already complete/tested; the real blockers were that **nothing was deployed** (GitHub Pages ships a backend-less SPA so relative `/api/v1/...` calls 404) and **public signup lacked email verification + forgot/reset**. **Phase 1 (backend):** migration 054 (`users.email_verified` grandfathered + hashed-token `email_verification_tokens`/`password_reset_tokens`); `lib/authTokens` + `lib/email` (console default, Resend `fetch` transport, fail-soft); `/register` issues+sends a verify token **post-commit** (never 500s); new `verify-email/{request,confirm}` (confirm auto-signs-in), `forgot-password`, `reset-password`; token failures are **400 `INVALID_TOKEN` never 401** (a 401 trips the global session-expiry logout); request endpoints always return generic `200 {sent:true}` (anti-enumeration); **soft gate** (login allowed unverified). 22/22 api tests, api `tsc` clean. **Phase 2 (frontend):** `apiClient`+`authStore` `emailVerified` + 4 actions; new public pages VerifyEmail/ForgotPassword/ResetPassword + routes; Forgot-password link; post-register note; web `tsc` 0, 11/11 touched web tests. **Phase 3 (Render):** `render.yaml` Blueprint (atlas-postgres PG16/PostGIS, atlas-redis keyvalue noeviction, private atlas-api with preDeploy migrate, public atlas-web nginx, domain atlas.ogden.ag); `Dockerfile.nginx` bakes SPA (`vite build` direct, skips Playwright prerender, 7168MB heap); `Dockerfile.api` migrations COPY fixed to `dist/db/migrations`; **new** `nginx/render-default.conf.template` (atlas-api upstream, `listen ${PORT}` envsubst, static `/healthz`, no certbot/443) **instead of mutating the dual-use compose `default.conf`** (⚠ deviation from plan, flagged in ADR); `deploy.yml` -> `.disabled`. render.yaml valid YAML; **docker builds NOT run** (daemon down -- operator validates on Render). **Phase 4:** `infrastructure/DEPLOY-RENDER.md` operator runbook. Single verified commit `b7388989` (27 files, +1628/-17), not pushed. Local e2e auth walkthrough + docker build gate deferred. ADR [[decisions/2026-06-05-atlas-live-auth-and-render-deploy]].
